================================================================================
 SphereNet Changelog
 Tum onemli degisiklikler bu dosyada belgelenir.
All notable changes are documented in this file.
================================================================================

[2026-05-28] - Yasam dongusu bypass ve client sync duzeltmeleri
              (Lifecycle bypass and client sync fixes)
----------------------------------------

MERKEZI YASAM DONGUSU API / CENTRAL LIFECYCLE API:
  - OnLifecycleKill delegate: Kill() dogrudan cagrisi ProcessDeath pipeline'ini
    (corpse, loot, trigger, ghost gecisi) atliyordu. Tum 7 call site (poison tick,
    trap, field, script KILL/SUICIDE, GM .SUICIDE, spell fallback) merkezi delegate
    uzerinden ProcessDeath'e yonlendirildi.
    (Direct Kill() calls bypassed ProcessDeath pipeline (corpse, loot, triggers,
    ghost transition). All 7 call sites routed through central delegate.)
  - OnLifecycleResurrect delegate: Resurrect() dogrudan cagrisi client sync'i
    (body restore, equipment re-equip, paketler) atliyordu. Tum 5 call site
    (resurrection spell, GM .HEAL self/target, script RESURRECT, sector RESPAWN)
    merkezi delegate uzerinden OnResurrect()'e yonlendirildi.
    (Direct Resurrect() calls bypassed client sync (body restore, equipment,
    packets). All 5 call sites routed through central delegate.)

OLUM VE DIRILIS / DEATH AND RESURRECTION:
  - NPC healer manifest kontrolu: Healer NPC'ler manifest olmamis (war mode
    degil) ghost'lari diriltiyordu. War mode kontrolu eklendi, manifest uyarisi
    gonderiliyor.
    (NPC healers resurrected non-manifested ghosts. War mode check added with
    manifest warning message.)
  - Bandage rez manifest/proximity/LOS: Healing ile diriltme manifest, 3 tile
    mesafe ve corpse line-of-sight kontrolu yapmiyordu. Uc kontrol de eklendi.
    (Bandage resurrection skipped manifest, proximity, and corpse LOS checks.
    All three validations added.)
  - PacketDeathStatus dirilis: Dirilis sonrasi death UI kapanmiyordu.
    OnResurrect'e PacketDeathStatus(ActionResurrect) eklendi.
    (Death UI not dismissed after resurrection. PacketDeathStatus(ActionResurrect)
    added to OnResurrect.)
  - Login dead state: Olu karakter ile login'de ghost body ve death UI
    gonderilmiyordu. EnterWorld'de IsDead kontrolu eklendi.
    (Login with dead character didn't send ghost body or death UI. IsDead check
    added to EnterWorld.)

TELEPORT VE CLIENT SYNC / TELEPORT AND CLIENT SYNC:
  - Recall spell sync: Recall buyusu MoveCharacter cagiriyordu ama client'a
    Resync/HandleMapChanged gonderilmiyordu. OnSpellTeleport delegate eklendi.
    (Recall spell called MoveCharacter without client Resync/HandleMapChanged.
    OnSpellTeleport delegate added.)
  - Teleport spell implementasyonu: Teleport buyusu hedef pozisyona isimlama
    yapiyordu ama yer hedefi (CastTargetPos) kullanilmiyordu. Dogru pozisyon
    okuma ve client sync eklendi.
    (Teleport spell used target position instead of ground target CastTargetPos.
    Correct position reading and client sync added.)
  - Moongate/telepad cross-map: OnTeleport callback'i map degisimini
    algilamiyordu. oldMap parametresi eklendi, cross-map icin HandleMapChanged,
    same-map icin Resync cagiriliyor.
    (OnTeleport callback didn't detect map changes. oldMap parameter added —
    HandleMapChanged for cross-map, Resync for same-map.)

KAPI SYNC / DOOR SYNC:
  - Late-joiner door state: Acik kapilarin durumu sonradan yaklasan
    oyunculara gonderilmiyordu. _knownDoorOverrides takibi ve
    SyncOpenMapStaticDoors ile gec katilimci sync'i eklendi.
    (Open door state not sent to players arriving later. _knownDoorOverrides
    tracking and SyncOpenMapStaticDoors late-joiner sync added.)
  - Ghost kapi kisitlamasi: Ghost'lar kapilari acabiliyordu. IsDead kontrolu
    eklendi.
    (Ghosts could open doors. IsDead check added.)
  - Kapi collision/persistence: Acik kapilar collision kontrolune dahil
    degildi ve sunucu restart'inda sifilaniyordu. WalkCheck entegrasyonu ve
    WorldSaver/WorldLoader door state persistence eklendi.
    (Open doors excluded from collision checks and reset on restart. WalkCheck
    integration and door state save/load added.)

PARITY DUZELTMELERI / PARITY FIXES:
  - Poison icon sync: StatFlags dogrudan atamasi (|= / &=~) MarkDirty
    cagirmiyordu, client'ta zehir iconu guncellenmiyordu. SetStatFlag/
    ClearStatFlag kullanildi.
    (Direct StatFlags assignment skipped MarkDirty — poison icon not updated
    on client. Switched to SetStatFlag/ClearStatFlag.)
  - Trade backpack refresh: Trade tamamlandiginda her iki tarafin cantalari
    guncellenmiyordu. RefreshBackpackContents ve partner refresh delegate'i
    eklendi.
    (Backpacks not refreshed for both parties after trade completion.
    RefreshBackpackContents and partner refresh delegate added.)
  - NPC melee skill interrupt: NPC saldirisi (melee/breath/throw) devam eden
    skill'i (ornegin bandage) kesintiye ugratmiyordu. HasActiveSkillPending
    kontrolu ve ActiveSkillAborted cagrisi eklendi (3 lokasyon).
    (NPC attacks (melee/breath/throw) didn't interrupt pending skills like
    bandage. HasActiveSkillPending check and ActiveSkillAborted invoke added
    at 3 locations.)

[2026-05-28] - Kapsamli guvenlik taramasi Wave 11 — 17 hata duzeltmesi
              (Comprehensive security audit Wave 11 — 17 bug fixes)
----------------------------------------

KRITIK / CRITICAL:
  - UidTable serial overflow: Interlocked.Increment int tasmasi 2.1B+ obje sonrasi
    gecersiz serial uretiyordu. MaxIndex (0x0FFFFFFF) siniri ve tasma korumasi eklendi.
    (Interlocked.Increment overflow produced invalid serials after 2.1B+ objects.
    MaxIndex guard and overflow protection added.)
  - HandleDialogCommand: DIALOG/SDIALOG komutu HandleDialogCommand cagiriyordu ama
    metod olustu—rulmamisti, build kirilmisti. Metod ve recursion depth limiti (4)
    eklendi.
    (DIALOG/SDIALOG called HandleDialogCommand which did not exist — build was broken.
    Method created with recursion depth limit of 4.)
  - Program.cs thread race: Console input thread _running=false iken basliyordu,
    thread aninda cikabiliyordu. _running=true startup'tan once set edildi.
    (Console input thread started with _running=false — thread could exit immediately.
    _running=true now set before thread start.)

BUYU VE SAVAS / SPELL AND COMBAT:
  - Dead target spell: Tekil hedefli buyuler olu karakterlere uygulanabiliyordu.
    TargDead flag'i olmayan buyuler artik olu hedefi reddediyor.
    (Single-target spells could be cast on dead characters. Spells without TargDead
    flag now reject dead targets.)
  - AoE range cap: Alan etkili buyu menzili skill ile sinir—siz buyuyordu.
    Maksimum 8 tile siniri eklendi.
    (Area spell range scaled unbounded with skill. Capped at 8 tiles.)
  - Frozen item use: Donmus karakterler item kullanabiliyordu (iksir, yemek, craft).
    StatFlag.Freeze kontrolu HandleItemUse'a eklendi.
    (Frozen characters could use items. StatFlag.Freeze check added to HandleItemUse.)

ENVANTER VE OBJE / INVENTORY AND OBJECT:
  - Container cycle detection: AddItem'a ContainsInSubtree ile dairesel referans
    tespiti eklendi (maxDepth=16).
    (Circular container reference detection added via ContainsInSubtree.)
  - Crafting resource loss: ConsumeResource kismi basarisizlikta bazi kaynaklar
    tuketilip item olusturulmuyordu. Tuketim dogrudan yapiliyor (oncesinde
    re-verify zaten var).
    (Partial ConsumeResource failure consumed some resources without creating item.
    Consumption now proceeds directly after re-verification.)

NETWORK VE PROTOKOL / NETWORK AND PROTOCOL:
  - NetState slot index: Negatif slot degerleri (slot < 0) kabul ediliyordu.
    Alt sinir kontrolu eklendi.
    (Negative slot values accepted in OnCharSelect. Lower bound check added.)
  - Huffman tree bounds: BuildServerDecompTree nextNode siniri yoktu.
    1024 node limiti eklendi.
    (BuildServerDecompTree had no bounds check on nextNode. 1024 node limit added.)
  - Book page bounds: HandleBookPage sayfa numarasi dogrulanmiyordu, sinirsiz
    tag olusturulabiliyordu. maxPages siniri eklendi.
    (HandleBookPage page number was unbounded — unlimited tags could be created.
    maxPages validation added.)

SPAWN VE TIMER / SPAWN AND TIMER:
  - Spawn count limit: SpawnComponent ve ItemSpawnComponent MaxCount 250 ile
    sinirlandirildi (onceden ushort.MaxValue=65535 mumkundu).
    (SpawnComponent and ItemSpawnComponent MaxCount capped at 250.)
  - TIMER negatif delay: Script TIMER komutu negatif deger kabul edip gecmiste
    timeout ayarlayabiliyordu. Math.Max(0, ...) eklendi.
    (Script TIMER command accepted negative values setting timeout in the past.
    Clamped to zero.)

DIGER / OTHER:
  - Resurrect MarkDirty: Dirilis sonrasi stat degisiklikleri client'a
    bildirilmiyordu. MarkDirty(StatFlags|Stats) eklendi.
    (Stat changes after resurrection not synced to client. MarkDirty added.)
  - Housing redeed: Redeed iki kez cagrildiginda cift silme olusuyordu.
    _redeeded idempotency flag'i eklendi.
    (Calling Redeed twice caused double deletion. Idempotency flag added.)
  - Housing lockdown: Ev siniri disindaki itemler lockdown yapilabiliyordu.
    FindHouseAt pozisyon dogrulamasi eklendi.
    (Items outside house bounds could be locked down. Position validation via
    FindHouseAt added.)
  - NEWITEM orphan: Disconnect'te _pendingScriptNewItem temizlenmeden
    birakiliyordu. RemoveItem ile temizleniyor.
    (Orphaned _pendingScriptNewItem not cleaned on disconnect. Now removed.)
  - Stable skill cap: Stable'a alinan pet skill degerleri 1000 ustunde
    olabiliyordu. Math.Min(sv, 1000) siniri eklendi.
    (Stabled pet skill values could exceed 1000. Capped at 1000.)

TESTLER / TESTS:
  - OnCharSelect_NegativeSlot testi yeni davranisa guncellendi (reject).
  - Login pipeline testleri slot=-1'den slot=0'a guncellendi.

[2026-05-28] - Kapsamli guvenlik ve oyun mantigi denetimi — 40+ hata duzeltmesi
              (Comprehensive security and game logic audit — 40+ bug fixes)
----------------------------------------

KRITIK GUVENLIK / CRITICAL SECURITY:
  - Vendor buy/sell: Client tarafindan gonderilen fiyat artik kullanilmiyor, sunucu
    tarafli fiyat hesaplamasi eklendi. Gold/item duplikasyonu onlendi.
    (Vendor buy/sell no longer trusts client-provided prices. Server-side price lookup
    prevents gold/item duplication exploits.)
  - HandleItemDrop: DRAGGING tag dogrulamasi eklendi. Oyuncular artik sadece
    surukladikleri itemi birakabiliyor, keyfi item tasima onlendi.
    (HandleItemDrop now validates DRAGGING tag. Players can only drop items they are
    actually dragging — arbitrary item movement prevented.)
  - WorldLoader OSTR/ODEX/OINT: Save/load dongusunde base stat'lar yanlis alana
    yukleniyor, karakter statlari her restart'ta bozuluyordu. Duzeltildi.
    (OSTR/ODEX/OINT were loaded into Str/Dex/Int instead of OStr/ODex/OInt,
    corrupting character stats every save/load cycle. Fixed.)
  - Guild title serialization: Colon iceren title'lar serializasyon formatini
    bozuyordu. Escape mekanizmasi eklendi.
    (Guild member titles containing colons corrupted serialization format.
    Colon escaping added.)
  - Housing stale tags: Kaldirilan co-owner/friend/ban/lockdown restart sonrasi
    geri geliyordu. Bos listeler artik RemoveTag ile temizleniyor.
    (Removed co-owners/friends/bans/lockdowns were restored after restart.
    Empty lists now cleaned via RemoveTag.)
  - Vendor buy item spam: Tek seferde 100 item alimi 100 ayri obje olusturuyordu.
    Artik tek stack olarak olusturuluyor (DoS onleme).
    (Buying 100 items created 100 separate objects. Now creates single stacked item.)
  - ProcessSell ushort truncation: 65535+ amount ile item duplikasyonu mumkundu.
    Amount siniri eklendi.
    (ProcessSell ushort cast allowed item duplication with amount > 65535. Fixed.)

OLUM VE SAVAS / DEATH AND COMBAT:
  - Poison death: Zehir hasari HP'yi 0'a dusurdugunde olum tetiklenmiyordu. Artik
    ProcessPoisonTick sonrasi Kill() cagriliyor.
    (Poison damage reducing HP to 0 did not trigger death. Kill() now called after
    ProcessPoisonTick when Hits <= 0.)
  - Spell curse stat underflow: Weaken/Clumsy/Feeblemind/Curse statlari negatife
    dusuruyordu, MaxHits/MaxMana/MaxStam bozuluyordu. Minimum 1 siniri eklendi.
    (Curse spells could reduce stats below zero, corrupting MaxHits/MaxMana/MaxStam.
    Stats now clamped to minimum 1.)
  - Blessed/Newbie item: Olumde Blessed/Blessed2/Newbie/Nodropt itemler artik
    cesede dusmeyip karakterde kaliyor.
    (Blessed/Blessed2/Newbie/Nodropt items now stay on character instead of falling
    to corpse on death.)
  - Death dismount: Olumde binek uzerindeyken dismount yapiliyordu.
    (Character now dismounted on death.)
  - Melee LOS: Yakin dovus saldirilarinda gorus hatti kontrolu eklendi.
    (Line-of-sight check added for melee attacks.)
  - Hidden staff attack: Gizli GM'lere normal oyuncular saldiramiyor.
    (Normal players can no longer attack hidden staff members.)

HAREKET VE POZISYON / MOVEMENT AND POSITION:
  - HandleMovementBatch: Onceki refactor sirasinda kirilan sanal zaman mekanizmasi
    geri yuklendi. Toplu hareket adimlarinin throttle tarafindan reddedilmesi onlendi.
    (Restored virtual-time mechanism broken during previous refactoring. Prevents
    batch movement steps from being throttle-rejected.)
  - Login Z correction: Ust katlardaki (cati, kopru, 2. kat) karakterler login'de
    yere snap'leniyordu. Math.Abs(diff) kontrolu ile duzeltildi.
    (Characters on upper floors were snapped to ground on login. Fixed with
    Math.Abs(diff) check preserving upper-floor positions.)
  - Stamina underflow: MovementEngine.CanShove Stam -= 10 negatife dusebiliyordu.
    Math.Max(0, ...) eklendi.
    (Stamina could go negative in CanShove. Clamped to 0.)

ENVANTER VE ITEM / INVENTORY AND ITEM:
  - Stack splitting: HandleItemPickup amount parametresi kullanilmiyordu.
    Artik stackable itemlarda miktar belirtildiginde split yapiliyor.
    (HandleItemPickup amount parameter was ignored. Stack splitting now works.)
  - Container nesting: Dairesel container ic ice koyma onlendi (A->B->A).
    IsInsideContainer kontrolu eklendi.
    (Circular container nesting prevented. IsInsideContainer check added.)
  - GetDeepContentCount: Derinlik limiti eklendi (maxDepth=16), stack overflow onlendi.
    (Depth limit added to prevent stack overflow.)
  - HandleItemDrop distance: Yere birakma icin 3 tile mesafe siniri eklendi.
    (3-tile distance limit added for ground drops.)
  - Vendor NPC range: Vendor etkilesimi icin 3 tile mesafe kontrolu eklendi.
    (3-tile distance check added for vendor interaction.)

HIRSIZLIK VE BECERI / STEALING AND SKILLS:
  - Stealing item dupe: Calinan item kaynak container'dan silinmiyordu, iki
    container'da ayni anda var oluyordu. RemoveItem cagrisi eklendi.
    (Stolen item was not removed from source container, existing in two containers
    simultaneously. RemoveItem call added.)
  - ResolveItemOwner: Sinirsiz recursion stack overflow'a neden olabiliyordu.
    Loop tabanli implementasyon (maxDepth=16) ile degistirildi.
    (Unbounded recursion could cause stack overflow. Replaced with loop-based
    implementation with maxDepth=16.)
  - Healing overflow: Sifa miktari MaxHits'i asabiliyordu. Clamp eklendi.
    (Heal amount could exceed MaxHits. Clamp added.)

HESAP VE GIRIS / ACCOUNT AND LOGIN:
  - PrivLevel escalation: Karakter PrivLevel'i account'u yukseltebiliyordu.
    Account artik otoritatif kaynak, karakter account'u yukseltemiyor.
    (Character PrivLevel could permanently elevate account. Account is now
    authoritative — character cannot elevate account privilege.)
  - Character name sanitization: Ozel karakter filtreleme ve 30 karakter siniri.
    (Special character filtering and 30-character limit added.)
  - PRIVLEVEL/FLAGS speech block: GM konusma komutlariyla PRIVLEVEL/PLEVEL/FLAGS
    degistirilemez.
    (PRIVLEVEL/PLEVEL/FLAGS cannot be set via GM speech commands.)

CRAFTING:
  - ConsumeResource dogrulama: Craft basari durumunda kaynaklar gump callback
    gecikmesi nedeniyle degismis olabiliyordu. Tuketim oncesi yeniden dogrulama ve
    tuketim sonucu kontrolu eklendi.
    (Resources may have changed between CanCraft and TryCraft due to gump callback
    delay. Re-verification before consumption and result checking added.)

PARTI VE GUILD / PARTY AND GUILD:
  - Party dual membership: AcceptInvite artik oyuncunun baska partide olup
    olmadigini kontrol ediyor.
    (AcceptInvite now checks if player is already in another party.)
  - Guild ElectMaster: Non-member'lara oy verilebiliyordu, masterless guild
    olusabiliyordu. Non-member adaylar filtreleniyor.
    (Voting for non-members could create masterless guilds. Non-member candidates
    now filtered.)
  - Guild stale tags: Charter, align, relations, wars, allies bos olunca tag
    temizleniyor.
    (Guild tags cleaned when charter/align/relations/wars/allies become empty.)

DIGER / OTHER:
  - Regen MarkDirty: HP/mana/stam rejen degisiklikleri client'a bildirilmiyordu.
    MarkDirty(DirtyFlag.Stats) eklendi. Mana INT-scaled, stam DEX-scaled yapildi.
    (HP/mana/stam regen changes not sent to client. MarkDirty added. Mana now
    INT-scaled, stam DEX-scaled.)
  - Meditation flag: Mana doldugunda Meditation flag temizleniyor.
    (Meditation flag cleared when mana reaches max.)
  - Red zone notoriety: Degerler ters donuyordu (katil=mavi, iyi=kirmizi). Duzeltildi.
    (Values were inverted — murderer returned blue, good karma returned red. Fixed.)
  - Dead NPC timer: Olu NPC'ler timer wheel'e tekrar planlanmiyordu.
    (Dead NPCs no longer rescheduled in the timer wheel.)
  - Context menu throttle: 500ms rate limiting eklendi.
    (500ms rate limiting added for context menu requests.)
  - PacketStatusFull buffer: 128 -> 200 byte, expansion level 7 icin yeterli.
    (Buffer increased from 128 to 200 bytes for expansion level 7.)
  - OnDisconnect cleanup: Pending target callback, input dialog, menu state
    temizleniyor.
    (Pending target callback, input dialog, menu state cleared on disconnect.)
  - Character.Delete() cleanup: Attacker/memory/target temizligi eklendi.
    (Attacker/memory/target cleanup added to Delete().)
  - WorldLoader skip property: Duplicate serial/UUID sonrasi deleted objelere
    property uygulanmasi onlendi.
    (Properties no longer applied to deleted objects after duplicate serial/UUID.)
  - Spawn tick overflow: delaySec * 1000L ile int overflow onlendi.
    (Spawn tick calculation uses 1000L to prevent int overflow.)
  - Party disconnect: Baglanti kopmasinda parti ayrilma islemi yapiliyor.
    (Party leave called on disconnect.)

[2026-05-26] - Merdiven/rampa Z desync duzeltmesi (teleport fix)
              (Stair/ramp Z desync correction — teleport fix)
----------------------------------------

Z CORRECTION MEKANIZMASI AKTIF:
  - WalkZCorrectionThreshold varsayilan deger 0'dan 4'e yukseltildi. Karakter merdiven
    veya rampada Z ekseni boyunca hareket ettiginde, birikimli Z kayma esik degeri asarsa
    sunucu MoveReject + MobileMoving gondererek client'i dogru pozisyona zorluyor. Onceden
    bu mekanizma devre disi oldugundan client kendi Z hesabini yapiyordu ve server ile
    uyumsuz kaldiginda karakter "teleport ediyormus gibi" gorunuyordu.
    (WalkZCorrectionThreshold default raised from 0 to 4. When character Z drifts beyond
    threshold on stairs/ramps, server sends MoveReject + MobileMoving to force client to
    correct position. Previously disabled — client computed Z independently, and when it
    disagreed with server the character appeared to "teleport".)

KONFIGURASYON / CONFIGURATION:
  - sphere.ini'den WalkZCorrectionThreshold ayarlanabilir. 0 = devre disi, 4 = varsayilan.
    Dusuk degerler daha sik duzeltme yapar (hassas), yuksek degerler daha az (toleransli).
    (Configurable via sphere.ini WalkZCorrectionThreshold. 0 = disabled, 4 = default.
    Lower values correct more aggressively, higher values are more tolerant.)

LOG DUZELTMESI / LOG FIX:
  - move_z_delta log satirinda kopya "ourZ" alani kaldirildi (fwdZ ile ayni degeri
    gosteriyordu).
    (Removed duplicate "ourZ" field from move_z_delta log line — it showed the same
    value as fwdZ.)

[2026-05-26] - Multi-client uyumluluk: per-client protokol negotiation
              (Multi-client compatibility: per-client protocol negotiation)
----------------------------------------

CLIENT TYPE TESPITI / CLIENT TYPE DETECTION:
  - 0xE1 ClientType flag'i artik gercekten kullaniliyor. Client 0=Classic2D, 1=3D,
    2=KR, 3=Enhanced olarak tanimlaniyor ve CLIENTISKR/IS3D/ISENHANCED script
    token'lari dogru sonuc donuyor. Onceden tum client'lar ClassicWindows varsayiliyordu.
    (0xE1 ClientType flag now actually used. Clients identified as Classic2D/3D/KR/Enhanced
    and CLIENTISKR/IS3D/ISENHANCED script tokens return correct results. Previously all
    clients were assumed ClassicWindows.)

PER-CLIENT FEATURE FLAG NEGOTIATION:
  - ServerFeatureFlags (sphere.ini) artik tavan degeri olarak kullaniliyor; her client'a
    gonderilen 0xB9 paketi client versiyonuna gore filtreleniyor. 7.0.9+ client full
    16-bit, 6.0.1.7+ client 8-bit, eski client'lar kendi kapasitelerine gore aliyorlar.
    Onceden admin flag set ettiginde tum client'lar ayni flag seti aliyordu.
    (ServerFeatureFlags now used as ceiling; 0xB9 feature enable packet filtered per
    client version. 7.0.9+ gets full 16-bit, 6.0.1.7+ gets 8-bit, older clients get
    their capacity. Previously all clients received identical flags when admin set them.)

EXPANSION FALLBACK:
  - Versiyon henuz tespit edilmemis client'lar (0xBD gelmeden) icin expansion=3 (AOS)
    baseline. Onceden expansion=0 (pre-AOS) donuyordu — tooltip ve item property'ler
    calismiyordu. Acikca pre-AOS (<4.0) olan client'lar hala expansion=0 aliyor.
    (Clients with undetected version now get AOS (expansion=3) baseline. Previously
    returned pre-AOS (0) breaking tooltips and item properties. Explicitly pre-AOS
    clients (<4.0) still receive expansion=0.)

0xF0 HAREKET PAKETI ROUTING / 0xF0 MOVEMENT PACKET ROUTING:
  - Batch vs single-step routing artik protokol versiyonu ve 0xE1 client type'a
    dayanarak karar veriyor. Onceden sadece payload boyutuna gore ayristiriliyordu
    (heuristic) — hybrid client'lar yanlis siniflandirilabiliyordu.
    (Batch vs single-step routing now uses protocol version and 0xE1 client type.
    Previously relied only on payload-size heuristic which could misclassify
    hybrid clients.)

VERSION FALLBACK IYILESTIRMESI / VERSION FALLBACK IMPROVEMENT:
  - KR/EC client'lar (0xE1 flag >= 2) 0xBD versiyon paketi gondermese bile en az 6.0
    olarak kabul ediliyor. Bu, container grid index, extended feature flag gibi 6.0+
    ozelliklerinin dogru calismasini sagliyor.
    (KR/EC clients (0xE1 flag >= 2) treated as at least 6.0 even without 0xBD version
    packet. Ensures 6.0+ features like container grid index and extended feature flags
    work correctly.)

TEST:
  - PacketNewMovementRequest_RoutesModernStepsAsBatch: SA+ client version set ediliyor
    (batch routing icin protocol detection gerekiyor).
    (Test updated: SA+ client version set for batch routing protocol detection.)

[2026-05-26] - Paperdoll isim/title duzeltmesi ve login paperdoll gonderimi
              (Paperdoll name/title fix and login paperdoll delivery)
----------------------------------------

PAPERDOLL DUZELTMESI / PAPERDOLL FIX:
  - DoubleClick (0x06) paketindeki bit 31 paperdoll flag'i artik dogru isleniyor.
    Client status bar'daki paperdoll butonu veya Alt+DoubleClick ile gelen istekler
    serial'in yuksek bit'i set edilmis olarak gelir — onceden bu serial karakter
    serial'iyla eslesmiyor ve paperdoll gonderilmiyordu.
    (DoubleClick packet (0x06) bit 31 paperdoll flag now handled correctly. Requests
    from the client status bar button or Alt+DClick send the serial with high bit set —
    previously this didn't match the character serial and no paperdoll was sent.)
  - EnterWorld login akisinda 0x88 paperdoll paketi gonderiliyor (Source-X paritesi).
    Bazi client'lar (ClassicUO, OrionUO, classic client) disconnect oncesi acik olan
    paperdoll penceresini login sonrasi geri yukler — artik isim/title verisi mevcut.
    (EnterWorld login flow now sends 0x88 paperdoll packet — Source-X parity. Some clients
    restore the paperdoll window on reconnect; name/title data is now available immediately.)
  - Paperdoll throttle (2sn) login gonderiminde de guncelleniyor — ayni karakter icin
    kisa surede tekrar paket gonderilmesini onluyor.
    (Paperdoll throttle (2s) updated on login send — prevents duplicate packet for same
    character within short timeframe.)

TEST:
  - EnterWorld_DoesNotAutoOpenPaperdoll -> EnterWorld_SendsPaperdollWithTitle olarak
    guncellendi (login'de 0x88 gonderimini dogruluyor).
    (Test renamed and updated to verify 0x88 is sent during login.)

[2026-05-26] - Combat animasyon/ses tamiri, hareket Z paritesi, guvenlik iyilestirmeleri
              (Combat animation/sound fixes, movement Z parity, security hardening)
----------------------------------------

COMBAT ANIMASYON / COMBAT ANIMATION:
  - Swing animasyonu damage hesabindan ONCE gonderiliyor; hit/miss her iki durumda
    silah kaldirma gorunur. Onceki davranista animasyon sadece hit yolunda ve damage
    sonrasinda gonderiliyordu — karakter silah kaldirmadan vuruyor gorunuyordu.
    (Swing animation now sent BEFORE damage resolution; weapon raise visible on both
    hit and miss. Previously animation was sent only in hit path after damage calc —
    character appeared to deal damage without swinging.)
  - Ranged projectile siralama: bow/xbow animasyonu artik ok/bolt ucmadan ONCE oynuyor.
    (Ranged projectile ordering: bow/xbow animation now plays BEFORE arrow/bolt flight.)
  - Mounted GetHit: at ustundeki target HorseSlap animasyonu aliyor (player yolunda eksikti).
    (Mounted GetHit: mounted target receives HorseSlap animation — was missing in player path.)
  - Miss yolunda artik sadece whoosh sesi (0x0234) gonderiliyor; swing anim zaten onceden gitti.
    (Miss path now sends only whoosh sound; swing anim already sent earlier.)
  - NPC BeginSwingRecoil: NPC'ler de artik swing state takip ediyor (CombatSwingState paritesi).
    (NPC BeginSwingRecoil: NPCs now track swing state via BeginSwingRecoil for state parity.)

MELEE HAREKET GECIKMESI / MELEE MOVEMENT DELAY:
  - CombatMeleeMovementDelay config secenegi (sphere.ini). Default 0 (devre disi).
    Ayarlandiginda koserken melee saldiri engellenir (archery delay'in melee karsiligi).
    (CombatMeleeMovementDelay config option. Default 0 (disabled). When set, blocks melee
    attacks while running — melee counterpart of CombatArcheryMovementDelay.)

    (Added IActiveSkillSink.Animation() — skills can now broadcast animations.)
  - Sound() broadcast fix: skill sesleri artik nearby herkese duyuluyor (onceden sadece self).
    (Sound() broadcast fix: skill sounds now heard by all nearby players, not just self.)
  - Healing (bandaj): Bow animasyonu + bandaj sesi (0x0057).

    (Container open: open sound.)

HAREKET Z PARITESI / MOVEMENT Z PARITY:

    Eski ServUO-style per-candidate IsOk yaklasimi yapisal farklar nedeniyle edge-case Z
    uyumsuzlugu uretiyordu. Yeni algoritma ClassicUO CalculateNewZ (Pathfinder.cs:370-512)
    ile birebir eslesir.
    (WalkCheck.Check() fully rewritten to ClassicUO sorted-list headroom algorithm. Old
    ServUO-style per-candidate IsOk approach produced edge-case Z divergence. New algorithm

[2026-05-26] - Network modernizasyonu: protokol altyapisi, guvenlik, hareket ve multi-era paket destegi

----------------------------------------

PROTOKOL / PROTOCOL:
  - ProtocolChanges enum (15 bayrak, Version500a - Version70610) ile client versiyon
    tespiti altyapisi eklendi; NetState uzerinde SupportsNewMobileIncoming,
    SupportsNewCharacterList, SupportsNewCharacterCreation, SupportsExtendedStatus
    helper property'leri tanimlandi.
    Added ProtocolChanges flags enum (15 flags from Version500a to Version70610) for
    client version detection; NetState gains per-version capability properties.
  - PacketDrawObject (0x78) versiyon dallanmasi: 7.0.33.1 oncesi 15-bit itemId + signal
    bit, 7.0.33.1+ 16-bit itemId + her zaman hue yazimi.
    PacketDrawObject (0x78) version branching: pre-7.0.33.1 uses 15-bit itemId with
    signal bit for hue, post-7.0.33.1 uses full 16-bit with hue always written.
  - PacketCharList (0xA9) versiyon dallanmasi: eski format 31-byte sehir alani,
    yeni format 32-byte + koordinat + trailing -1.
    PacketCharList (0xA9) version branching: old format 31-byte city fields without
    coords, new format 32-byte with coords and trailing -1.
  - ExtendedStatus (0x11) expansion seviyesi 7.0.30+ client'lar icin expansion=7
    olarak guncellendi; onceki ML client'lari expansion=5 almaya devam eder.
    ExtendedStatus (0x11) expansion level updated to 7 for clients 7.0.30+; older ML
    clients still receive expansion=5.
  - BroadcastDrawObject per-observer dispatch: ForEachClientInRange ile her gozlemciye
    kendi client versiyonuna uygun 0x78 formati gonderilir.
    BroadcastDrawObject refactored to per-observer dispatch via ForEachClientInRange,
    sending version-appropriate 0x78 format to each observer.
  - 0xF0 movement batch paketi parse ve handler eklendi; birden fazla walk adimi tek
    pakette islenir.
    Added 0xF0 movement batch packet parsing and handler; multiple walk steps are
    processed from a single packet.

    listesi (IPBlockList) eklendi; SphereConfig uzerinden yapilandirilabilir.

    via SphereConfig.
  - Sifre dogrulama SHA256 hash destegi eklendi (PasswordHelper); hesap sifreleri
    artik hash'lenerek saklanabilir.
    Password verification now supports SHA256 hashing via PasswordHelper; account
    passwords can be stored hashed.
  - 0xF0 batch paketi boyut ve step sayisi sinirlari eklendi (max 4096 byte,
    max 128 adim).
    0xF0 batch packet size and step count limits added (max 4096 bytes, 128 steps).

    yenileme ile hiz hilesi tespiti; CircularBuffer tabanli hareket gecmisi.
    Token-bucket credit system with burst buffer and per-second regen for speed hack
    detection; CircularBuffer-based movement history tracking.

[2026-05-24] - Guvenlik taramasi ve exploit duzeltmeleri
              (Security audit and exploit fixes)
----------------------------------------

KRITIK / CRITICAL:
  - TradeEngine vendor alis totalCost int overflow: Price*Amount carpimindan
    kaynaklanan negatif sarilma gold kontrolunu bypass ediyordu (gold dupe exploit).
    long aritmetik ve int.MaxValue cap eklendi.
    Vendor buy totalCost int overflow allowed negative wrap bypassing gold check.
    Fixed with long arithmetic and int.MaxValue cap.

GUVENLIK / SECURITY:
  - TelnetConsole _lineBuffer sinirsiz buyumesi engellendi (8KB cap); uzak DoS
    saldirisi ile bellek tukenmesi onlendi.
    TelnetConsole line buffer capped at 8KB to prevent remote OOM DoS.
  - Speech paketi Unicode metin uzunlugu 256 karakterle sinirlandirildi.
    Speech packet Unicode text capped at 256 characters.
  - CharSelect (0x5D) slotIndex bounds kontrolu eklendi (0-7 arasi).
    CharSelect slot index validated to [0,7] range.

SCRIPT / SCRIPT:
  - ExpressionParser ResolveAngleBrackets recursion derinlik limiti (max 32);
    TAG.X → TAG.Y → TAG.X gibi dongusel referanslar sonsuz dongu yaratamaz.
    Variable resolution recursion capped at depth 32 to prevent infinite loops.
  - ForObjects (FORCHARS, FORITEMS vb.) MaxLoopIterations kontrolu eklendi;
    buyuk obje listeleri uzerinde script DoS onlendi.
    ForObjects loops now respect MaxLoopIterations cap.
  - STRREGEX pattern uzunlugu 512, input 4096 karakterle sinirlandirildi;
    regex timeout 25ms'ye dusuruldu (ReDoS azaltma).
    STRREGEX pattern/input length capped and timeout reduced to 25ms.

HAREKET / MOVEMENT:
  - WalkCheck diagonal yonlerde negatif koordinat sinir kontrolu eklendi;
    harita kenarinda capraz yuruyus ile map-escape onlendi.
    WalkCheck diagonal boundary validation added for negative coordinates.

  - WorldLoader item self-containment kontrolu (CONT=kendi serial'i);
    dongusel container referanslari tespit edilip yere birakilir.
    Self-referencing item containers detected and placed on ground during load.

  - IniParser comment strip sonrasi bos satir guard eklendi.
    IniParser empty line guard added after comment stripping.

[2026-05-02] - GM komut paritesi: CURE, POISON, REVEAL, GOUID, GOCHAR, OPENPAPERDOLL, SHOWSKILLS, PAGE routing
              (GM command parity: CURE, POISON, REVEAL, GOUID, GOCHAR, OPENPAPERDOLL, SHOWSKILLS, PAGE routing)
----------------------------------------

GM KOMUTLARI / GM COMMANDS:
  - CURE: Hedef karakterin zehrini temizler. Argumansiz = kendine, UID ile = hedefe.
    Cures target's poison. No args = self, UID arg = target.
  - POISON: Hedefe 1-5 seviye zehir uygular. UID + seviye veya sadece seviye.
    Applies poison level 1-5 to target. UID + level or level only.
  - REVEAL: Hedefin Hidden/Invisible flaglerini kaldirir.
    Clears target's Hidden/Invisible stat flags.

TELEPORT ARAMA / TELEPORT SEARCH:
  - GOUID: Serial (hex/dec) ile objeye teleport. Source-X GOUID paritesi.
    Teleport to object by serial (hex/dec). Source-X GOUID parity.
  - GOCHAR: Isim aramasiyla karaktere teleport. Source-X GOCHAR paritesi.
    Teleport to character by name search. Source-X GOCHAR parity.

UI KOMUTLARI / UI COMMANDS:
  - OPENPAPERDOLL: Hedefin paperdoll'unu GM'de acar. UID ile veya argumansiz = kendi.
    Opens target's paperdoll on GM client. UID arg or no args = self.
  - SHOWSKILLS: GM'e skill listesi gonderir.
    Sends skill list to GM client.

PAGE YONLENDIRME / PAGE ROUTING:
  - .PAGE artik online Counsel+ staff'a SysMessage olarak yonlendiriliyor.
    .PAGE now routes to online Counsel+ staff via SysMessage broadcast.
  - Staff yoksa oyuncuya bilgi mesaji gosteriliyor, tum page'ler loglanıyor.
    If no staff online, player gets a notification. All pages are logged.
  - Argumansiz kullanim icin usage mesaji eklendi.
    Added usage message for empty args.

  - Paperdoll flag dinamik hesaplaniyor: bit 0x01 = warmode (hedef karakterden),

    bit 0x02 = dress permission (own paperdoll).

[2026-04-29] - NPC AI engine: akilli buyu secimi, melee taktik, healer/guard/vendor/witness
              (NPC AI engine: intelligent spellcasting, melee tactics, healer/guard/vendor/witness)
----------------------------------------

AKILLI BUYU SECIMI / INTELLIGENT SPELL SELECTION:
  - Rastgele buyu secimi yerine ChooseBestSpell: oncelik sirasi self-cure (zehir),
    self-heal (HP<%50), dispel (summon hedef), area spell (3+ dusman), paralyze,
    poison, yuksek hasar, debuff, fallback. Magic Reflect kontrolu.
    ChooseBestSpell replaces random spell pick: priority self-cure (poison),
    self-heal (HP<50%), dispel (summoned target), area spells (3+ enemies),
    paralyze, poison, high damage, debuffs, fallback. Magic Reflect awareness.
  - Heal dongusu onleme: self-heal %33 (kritik %50), cure %50 sansla — NPC hem
    iyilesir hem saldiriya devam eder, sonsuz heal dongusu olmaz.
    Heal loop prevention: self-heal 33% (critical 50%), cure 50% chance — NPC
    heals and attacks in mix, no infinite heal loop.

MELEE TAKTIK SISTEMI / MELEE TACTICS SYSTEM:
  - Kusatma/cevreleme: hedefin yanina yaklasirken (dist<=3) acik yonden flank,
    vurustan sonra (%33) hedefin etrafinda bos tile'a surround adimi.
    Surround/flank: approach from open flank (dist<=3), post-attack sidestep
    (33% chance) to unoccupied tile around target.
  - HP-based taktik geri cekilme: HP<%25 melee NPC bitisikteyken %33 ihtimalle
    bir adim geri cekilip sonraki tick'te tekrar saldiriyor.
    HP-based tactical retreat: HP<25% melee NPC at dist=1, 33% chance to step
    back then re-engage next tick.
  - Akilli hedef onceliklendirme: yarali hedef +15, caster NPC +10, healer NPC +20,
    bize saldiran hedef +15 motivasyon bonusu.
    Smart target prioritization: wounded target +15, caster NPC +10, healer NPC +20,
    retaliating target +15 motivation bonus.
  - Grup vurus dagilimi: swing delay'e UID-based 0-200ms offset — ayni hedefe
    saldiran NPC'ler farkli zamanlarda vuruyor.
    Group attack stagger: UID-based 0-200ms offset on swing delay — NPCs attacking
    same target swing at different times.

GELISMIS KACIS / IMPROVED FLEE:
  - Pathfinder-based kacis: ters yon bloklaninca alternatif diagonal yonler deniyor.
    Pathfinder-based flee: tries diagonal alternatives when direct retreat is blocked.
  - Kacis sirasinda buyu atma (kiting): her 3 adimda saldiri buyusu, her 4 adimda
    self-heal (HP<%33).
    Spell kiting while fleeing: offensive spell every 3rd step, self-heal every 4th
    step (HP<33%).

MUTTEFIK CAGRISI / ALLY CALL FOR HELP:
  - NotifyNearbyAllies: monster yeni hedef buldugunda 8 tile icindeki ayni BodyId'li
    NPC'ler kavgaya katiliyor.
    NotifyNearbyAllies: when a monster acquires a target, same-BodyId NPCs within
    8 tiles join the fight.

  - Menzil 3 → 5 tile. Healer uzaktaki olulere dogru yuruyor.
    Range 3 → 5 tiles. Healer walks toward distant dead players.
  - Yeni oncelik: resurrect > cure poison > heal (zehir tedavisi eklendi).
    New priority: resurrect > cure poison > heal (poison cure added).

[2026-04-26] - NEW.* property routing, ATTR hex parsing, container pozisyonlama
              (NEW.* property routing, ATTR hex parsing, container positioning)
----------------------------------------

SCRIPT ENGINE — NEW.* PROPERTY ROUTING:
  - SERV.NEWITEM sonrasi NEW.TYPE, NEW.ATTR, NEW.P, NEW.MORE, NEW.TIMER gibi
    tum property'ler artik TrySetProperty uzerinden route ediliyor.
    Onceden sadece NEW.EQUIP, NEW.CONT, NEW.AMOUNT taniniyor, diger
    property'ler sessizce atiliyordu — spawn item'ler map'e yerlesmiyordu.
    After SERV.NEWITEM, all NEW.* properties (TYPE, ATTR, P, MORE, TIMER, etc.)
    now route through TrySetProperty. Previously only NEW.EQUIP, NEW.CONT,
    NEW.AMOUNT were handled — other properties were silently dropped, so spawn
    items never got placed on the map.
  - NEW.CONT artik serial arguman ile belirli bir container'a da koyabiliyor.
    NEW.CONT now accepts a serial argument to place into a specific container.
  - Item TYPE setter artik "t_spawn_char" gibi type name'leri kabul ediyor.
    Item TYPE setter now accepts type name strings like "t_spawn_char".

ATTR HEX PARSING:
  - ATTR=0B0 gibi Source-X hex degerler artik dogru parse ediliyor.
    Eski kod sadece decimal (uint.TryParse) kullaniyordu, hex basarisiz oluyordu
    — spawn item'ler ATTR_INVIS alamiyordu, GM AllShow ile gorunmuyordu.
    Source-X hex values like ATTR=0B0 now parse correctly. Old code used
    decimal-only uint.TryParse — hex values failed silently, so spawn items
    never got ATTR_INVIS and were invisible even to GM AllShow.
  - ParseHexOrDecUInt ObjBase'e tasindi, tum alt siniflar kullaniyor.
    ParseHexOrDecUInt moved to ObjBase, shared by all subclasses.

CONTAINER ITEM POZISYONLAMA / CONTAINER ITEM POSITIONING:
  - AddItem artik container gump sinirlari icinde random X,Y pozisyonu atiyor.
    Onceden tum item'ler X=0,Y=0 ile gump'in gorunur alaninin disinda kaliyordu.
    AddItem now assigns random X,Y within container gump bounds. Previously all
    items got X=0,Y=0 which falls outside the visible gump area.
  - Source-X GetRandContainerLoc ile tam uyumlu: TDATA3/TDATA4 custom bounds
    destegi, yoksa gump ID bazli hardcoded bounds tablosu (60+ gump).
    Full parity with Source-X GetRandContainerLoc: TDATA3/TDATA4 custom bounds
    support, with hardcoded gump bounds table fallback (60+ gumps).

REGION CACHE PERFORMANS / REGION CACHE PERFORMANCE:
  - FindRegion artik 8x8 tile grid bazli ConcurrentDictionary cache kullaniyor.
    O(n) full scan eliminasyonu — her tick binlerce FindRegion cagrisi icin.
    FindRegion now uses an 8x8 tile grid ConcurrentDictionary cache.
    Eliminates O(n) full scan — critical for thousands of FindRegion calls/tick.
  - Region.TotalArea cached property: alan hesabi tekrar tekrar yapilmiyor.
    Region.TotalArea cached property: area calculation no longer repeated.

EKSIK SCRIPT PROPERTY'LERI / MISSING SCRIPT PROPERTIES:
  - Character: WEIGHT (recursive agirlik), RANGE (weapon ItemDef'ten),
    CANSEELOS.uid, CANSEE.uid, FINDUID.uid
  - Item: TOPOBJ (top-level container/character)
  - ObjBase: ISTEVENT.defname / ISEVENT.defname
  - REGION.* artik tum Region property'lerine delege ediyor (eski: sadece NAME/UID)
    REGION.* now delegates to Region.TryGetProperty for all props (was: NAME/UID only)

[2026-04-25h] - Tick pipeline performans optimizasyonu (tick pipeline performance tuning)
----------------------------------------

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - FindRegion eliminasyonu: NPC hareket (MoveCharacter) her cagriyi 2x FindRegion
    (tum AREADEF linear scan) yapiyordu. NPC'ler icin tamamen kaldirildi, sadece
    IsPlayer ise calisir. 11.500 NPC move/tick icin ~435ms kazanc.
    FindRegion elimination: MoveCharacter called FindRegion twice per move (full
    AREADEF linear scan). Skipped entirely for NPCs, runs only for IsPlayer.
    ~435ms savings for 11,500 NPC moves/tick.
  - Allocation churn eliminasyonu: ConcurrentBag → lock+List.Add,
    ConcurrentDictionary → reusable static, refreshClients → reusable static.
    Her tick'te sifir GC allokasyonu.
    Allocation churn elimination: ConcurrentBag → lock+List.Add,
    ConcurrentDictionary → reusable static, refreshClients → reusable static.
    Zero GC allocation per tick.
  - Bos sektor atlama: OnCharacterMoved, BroadcastCharacterAppear,
    MarkNearbyClientsRefresh icinde OnlinePlayers.Count==0 kontrolu ile bos
    sektorler hicbir islem yapilmadan atlaniyor.
    Empty sector skip: OnCharacterMoved, BroadcastCharacterAppear,
    MarkNearbyClientsRefresh skip sectors with OnlinePlayers.Count==0 —
    no enumerator created for empty sectors.
  - NPC karar siralama kaldirildi: Apply fazinda UID sirasina gore sort
    gereksizdi, ~0.2ms kazanc.
    NPC decision sort removed: UID-ordered sort in apply phase was unnecessary,
    ~0.2ms savings.
  - NPC hareket zamanlama yayilimi: Timer wheel burst'u azaltmak icin
    sabit 200ms jitter yerine UID-tabanli 400ms faz ofseti. Ayni ortalama
    periyot (~800ms), tick basina ~2x daha az NPC patlamasi.
    NPC move timing spread: UID-based 400ms phase offset instead of fixed
    200ms jitter to reduce timer wheel bursts. Same average period (~800ms),
    ~2x fewer NPCs per tick burst.

  Sonuc / Result:
    Once (100 bot):  avg=547ms  max=639ms
    Sonra (300 bot): avg=53.6ms max=146ms  (~10x iyilesme, 3x fazla yuk)
    Before (100 bots): avg=547ms  max=639ms
    After (300 bots):  avg=53.6ms max=146ms (~10x improvement, 3x more load)

TANI / DIAGNOSTICS:
  - Compute fazini 4 alt olcume bolme: slow_tick logu artik npc_build,
    client_state, npc_apply, view_build ayrimini gosteriyor.
    Compute phase 4-way breakdown: slow_tick log now shows npc_build,
    client_state, npc_apply, view_build split.
  - .SECTORLIST komutu: Online player'larin bulundugu sektorleri, NPC/item/player
    sayilariyla scrollable HTML dialog olarak gosterir. NPC yogunluguna gore
    renk kodlu. Counsel+ erisim.
    .SECTORLIST command: shows sectors with online players in a scrollable HTML
    dialog with NPC/item/player counts. Color-coded by NPC density. Counsel+ access.

[2026-04-25f] - Nesne merkezli gorunum yayini (object-centric view broadcasting)
----------------------------------------

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - Client-centric BuildViewDelta her tick'te TUM client'lar icin calismak yerine
    sadece ViewNeedsRefresh isaretli client'lar icin calisiyor. 1000 oyuncu
    senaryosunda cogu client idle oldugundan %90+ BuildViewDelta cagrisini atliyor.
    Client-centric BuildViewDelta now runs only for ViewNeedsRefresh-flagged clients
    instead of ALL clients every tick. With 1000 players, most clients are idle,
    skipping 90%+ of BuildViewDelta calls.
  - NPC hareketi artik CharacterMoved event uzerinden aninda yakinlardaki client'lara
    bildiriliyor (enter-range 0x78, leave-range 0x1D, position-update 0x77).
    BuildViewDelta'ya gerek kalmadan O(hareket_eden_NPC × yakin_client) maliyetle.
    NPC movement now broadcasts instantly to nearby clients via CharacterMoved event
    (enter-range 0x78, leave-range 0x1D, position-update 0x77) at O(moved_NPCs ×
    nearby_clients) cost, bypassing BuildViewDelta entirely.
  - Oyuncu hareketi: kendi client'i ViewNeedsRefresh isaretleniyor (viewport item
    guncellemeleri icin), diger client'lar icin enter/leave-range aninda isleniyor.
    BroadcastMoveNearby mevcut 0x77 yayinini yapmayi surduruyor.
    Player movement: own client flagged ViewNeedsRefresh (for viewport item updates),
    other clients get instant enter/leave-range handling. BroadcastMoveNearby
    continues handling the existing 0x77 broadcast for known characters.
  - Dirty objeler (body/hue/equip degisiklikleri) yakinlardaki client'lari
    ViewNeedsRefresh ile isaretliyor — tum client'lar yerine sadece etkilenenler
    guncelleniyor.
    Dirty objects (body/hue/equip changes) mark nearby clients via ViewNeedsRefresh —
    only affected clients run view updates instead of all.
  - Item olusturma/silinme olaylari yakinlardaki client'lari otomatik isaretliyor.
    Item creation/deletion events automatically flag nearby clients for refresh.
  - Fast-path (tick arasi dirty guncelleme) de ayni ViewNeedsRefresh mekanizmasini
    kullaniyor — idle client'lar hicbir sekilde isleme alinmiyor.
    Fast-path (between-tick dirty updates) also uses ViewNeedsRefresh mechanism —
    idle clients are never processed.
  - Sektor bazli OnlinePlayers takibi: tum broadcast/notify donguleri artik
    sector.Characters (NPC dahil) yerine sector.OnlinePlayers iterate ediyor.
    100K NPC'li sektorlerde oyuncu aramak icin yuzlerce karakter yerine sadece
    0-2 online oyuncu taraniyor.
    Sector-based OnlinePlayers tracking: all broadcast/notify loops now iterate
    sector.OnlinePlayers instead of sector.Characters (which includes NPCs).
    Finding players in sectors with 100K NPCs scans only 0-2 online players
    instead of hundreds of characters.
  - NPC olusturma/silinme artik BroadcastCharacterAppear ile aninda yakinlardaki
    client'lara bildiriliyor (stress/spawn ile NPC olusan ama gorunmeyen bug fix).
    NPC creation/deletion now instantly notifies nearby clients via
    BroadcastCharacterAppear (fixes invisible NPCs from stress/spawn).

MIMARI / ARCHITECTURE:
  - GameWorld.CharacterMoved event: MoveCharacter artik eski pozisyonu yakalayip
    event atesledigi icin dinleyiciler enter/leave-range hesabi yapabiliyor.
    GameWorld.CharacterMoved event: MoveCharacter now captures old position and fires
    event, enabling listeners to compute enter/leave-range.
  - GameClient.ViewNeedsRefresh: client bazinda flag, hareket veya yakin obje
    degisikliginde set ediliyor. Sadece isaretli client'lar BuildViewDelta + Apply
    dongusu calistiriyor.
    GameClient.ViewNeedsRefresh: per-client flag set on movement or nearby object
    changes. Only flagged clients run BuildViewDelta + Apply cycle.
  - GameClient.NotifyCharMoved: NPC hareketi icin aninda enter/leave/update islemi.
    GameClient.NotifyCharEnterLeave: oyuncu hareketi icin sadece enter/leave
    (still-in-range BroadcastMoveNearby tarafindan isleniyor).
    GameClient.NotifyCharMoved: instant enter/leave/update for NPC movement.
    GameClient.NotifyCharEnterLeave: enter/leave only for player movement
    (still-in-range handled by BroadcastMoveNearby).
  - Resync() artik ViewNeedsRefresh=true set ediyor — login/teleport sonrasi tam
    gorunum yenilemesi garantileniyor.
    Resync() now sets ViewNeedsRefresh=true — guarantees full view refresh after
    login/teleport.

[2026-04-25e] - NPC sektor uyku ve AI throttle optimizasyonu
----------------------------------------

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - Sektor bazli O(1) aktif alan kontrolu: IsInActiveArea artik her NPC icin
    tum online oyunculari iterate etmiyor (O(players)), bunun yerine NPC'nin
    sektorunun aktif sette olup olmadigini HashSet lookup ile kontrol ediyor (O(1)).
    100K NPC + 100 oyuncu senaryosunda ~333K mesafe hesabi → ~3K HashSet lookup.
    Sector-based O(1) active area check: IsInActiveArea no longer iterates all
    online players per NPC (O(players)), instead checks sector membership via
    HashSet lookup (O(1)). 100K NPCs + 100 players: ~333K distance checks → ~3K
    HashSet lookups.
  - Uyuyan NPC park suresi 5-10s'den 30-60s'e cikarildi: Timer wheel churn'u ~6x
    azalir — her tick'te pop edilen NPC sayisi dramatik olarak duser.
    Sleeping NPC park time increased from 5-10s to 30-60s: timer wheel churn
    reduced ~6x — dramatically fewer NPCs popped per tick.
  - Sektor uyanma mekanizmasi: Oyuncu yeni bir bolgee girdiginde o sektorun
    NPC'leri aninda uyandirilir (timer wheel'e 100ms ile yeniden zamanlanir).
    30-60s park suresi NPC tepkisini geciktirmez.
    Sector wake mechanism: when a player enters a new area, that sector's NPCs
    are immediately woken (rescheduled to 100ms in timer wheel). The 30-60s park
    time does not delay NPC responsiveness.
  - Aktif sektor seti tek noktadan yonetiliyor: Hem single-thread hem multicore
    tick yolu ayni RefreshActiveSectors() metodunu cagiriyor. Yeni uyanan sektorler
    (NewlyActiveSectors) her iki yolda da tespit ediliyor.
    Active sector set managed from single point: both single-thread and multicore
    tick paths call the same RefreshActiveSectors(). Newly woken sectors detected
    in both paths.

[2026-04-25d] - State recording performans optimizasyonu
----------------------------------------

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - StateRecorder async flush: Hareket ve snapshot verileri ConcurrentQueue ile
    toplanir, ayri bir arka plan thread'inde SQLite'a toplu yazilir. Oyun thread'i
    artik disk I/O beklemez.
    StateRecorder async flush: movement and snapshot data collected via ConcurrentQueue,
    batch-written to SQLite on a dedicated background thread. Game thread no longer
    blocks on disk I/O.
  - Players-only filtre: StateRecordPlayersOnly=1 (varsayilan) ile sadece oyuncu
    karakterleri taranir — 100K NPC'li dunya icin gereksiz iterasyon ortadan kalkar.
    Players-only filter: StateRecordPlayersOnly=1 (default) scans only player
    characters — eliminates unnecessary iteration for worlds with 100K+ NPCs.
  - Yapilandirilabilir tarama araliklari: StateRecordMoveScanMs (varsayilan 2000ms)
    ve StateRecordSnapshotMs (varsayilan 15000ms) ayarlari sphere.ini uzerinden
    degistirilebilir. Eski sabit degerler (500ms/10s) yerine daha az CPU yuku.
    Configurable scan intervals: StateRecordMoveScanMs (default 2000ms) and
    StateRecordSnapshotMs (default 15000ms) adjustable via sphere.ini. Less CPU
    overhead compared to old hardcoded values (500ms/10s).
  - ThreadPool-dispatched cleanup: Eski kayitlarin temizlenmesi ThreadPool'a
    devredilir, oyun thread'ini bloklamaz.
    ThreadPool-dispatched cleanup: old record purging dispatched to ThreadPool,
    does not block game thread.

    (skill ID), TargetLocation (ground target), TargetObject (object target),
    TargetSelf. Delays between steps automatically captured during recording.

    varsayilan 50), MacroMaxLoopMinutes (maks loop suresi, varsayilan 120 dk).
    sphere.ini uzerinden yapilandirilabilir.

    default 50), MacroMaxLoopMinutes (max loop duration, default 120 min).
    Configurable via sphere.ini.

    derinlikte) ve kuşanılmış ekipmanda item tipine göre arar. Item bulunamazsa
    makro otomatik durur.
    Smart item lookup: during playback UseObject step searches backpack (2 levels deep)
    and equipped items by type. Macro auto-stops if item not found.
  - Target bekleme mekanizmasi: Playback sirasinda target cursor henuz acilmamissa
    5 saniyeye kadar bekler, timeout olursa adimi atlar.
    Target wait mechanism: during playback if target cursor not yet open, waits up to
    5 seconds, skips step on timeout.

[2026-04-21] - PrivLevel save tutarsizligi #2: load-time reconcile, max-tabanli login senkronu

DUZELTMELER / FIXES:
  - Program.ReconcileAccountCharPrivLevels: World ve account dosyalari
    yuklendikten hemen sonra (henuz hicbir client baglanmadan) calisan
    tek seferlik bir bos vardiya ekledi. Her hesabin CHARUID slot'lari
    geziliyor, slot'taki karakter bulunduktan sonra
    max(account.PrivLevel, char.PrivLevel) iki tarafa da yaziliyor.
    Boylece "char=GM, account=Player" ya da "account=Owner, char=Player"
    gibi miras kalmis bozuk save kombinasyonlari ilk login'den onuglu
    bellekte tutarli hale geliyor; sonraki dunya save'i hem spherechars
    hem sphereaccu'ya max degeri yaziyor. Mismatch bulununca ayrica
    "PrivLevel mismatch: account=... char=... Promoting both to ..."
    log satiri uretiliyor, repair sayisi info olarak ozetleniyor.
    One-shot reconciliation pass after world+account load: walks each
    account's char slots and promotes both sides to max(account, char).
    Heals legacy "char=GM/account=Player" or "account=Owner/char=Player"
    desyncs in memory before any client connects; the next save persists
    the corrected pair to disk. Logs each repair plus a one-line summary.
  - GameClient.EnterWorld PrivLevel sync: Eski "char>account ise hesabi
    yukselt, aksi halde karakteri hesaptan indir" kuralinin yerine
    simetrik max kuralina cevrildi. Kucuk olan taraf otomatik olarak
    buyuk olana esitleniyor, hicbir taraf bir digerini demote etmiyor.
    Mismatch durumunda "[LOGIN] PrivLevel sync: account=... PLEVEL=...
    char=... PRIVLEVEL=... -> X" diagnostik log satiri basiliyor; sync
    gereksizse log da basilmiyor. Boot reconcile zaten ayni i$i bir kez
    daha yaptigi icin bu blok ek savunma katmani; her iki yol birden
    devre disi kalmadikca PrivLevel demote olmuyor.
    EnterWorld sync rewritten as symmetric max(account, char) — neither
    side ever demotes the other. Mismatch logs the before/after for
    debuggability; identical levels stay silent.

    Karakterin disk'ten yuklenen PrivLevel'i (spherechars/PRIVLEVEL)
    hesabin PLEVEL'inden buyukse hesap karakter seviyesine yukseltiliyor;
    aksi halde klasik "hesap otorite" yon korunuyor (admin tarafindan
    account uzerinden indirme calismaya devam ediyor). Eski .privset /
    .privlevel yollari hesabi guncellemeden karakteri yukselttigi icin
    diskte PRIVLEVEL=GM + PLEVEL=Player kayitlari olusmustu; her
    girisinde bu satir karakteri tekrar Player'a indiriyor, "oyuna

    bozulmus mevcut kayitlari ilk girisinde iyilestiriyor; sonraki dunya
    save'i iki tarafi da tutarli yaziyor.
    EnterWorld now reconciles char/account PrivLevel both ways: if the
    saved character outranks the account, the account is promoted to the
    character's level (heals legacy snapshots), otherwise the account
    stays authoritative. Fixes "PLEVEL resets to 1 on login" caused by
    older .privset / PRIVLEVEL paths that wrote char.PRIVLEVEL without
    mirroring acc.PLEVEL; one login restores parity and the next save
    persists both sides consistently.
  - Character.TryExecuteCommand PRIVSET: Komut artik _privLevel alanina
    dogrudan yazmak yerine PrivLevel property setter'i uzerinden
    geciyor. Setter zaten _isPlayer kontrolu + ResolveAccountForChar ile
    bagli hesabin PLEVEL'ini de mirror ediyordu; PRIVSET de artik bu
    yolu kullandigi icin oyun-ici PrivLevel degisiklikleri tek save
    cyclu'nde hem spherechars hem sphereaccu'ya tutarli yaziliyor ve
    bir daha ayni driftin ureyemiyor.
    PRIVSET verb routes through the PrivLevel property setter instead
    of writing _privLevel directly, so the account-side mirror runs and
    every in-game privilege change is persisted on both save files in a
    single cycle — preventing the inconsistency from re-emerging.

  - DebugUnresolved varsayilan olarak KAPALI birakildi. Acik bir surede
    her cozumlenmemis <X> bir string-format + log yazimi maliyetine
    sebep oluyor; gurultulu script paketleri (NPC tick, region tick)
    saniyede binlerce uyari uretebiliyor. .SCRIPTDEBUG ON sadece eksik
    property/defname avlarken kullanilmali, production'da kapali kalmali.
    Inline doc string'i bu konuda uyari ekleyecek sekilde guncellendi.
    DebugUnresolved stays off by default; enabling it under load is
    expensive (every unresolved <X> pays a string-format + log write),
    so the docstring now warns against leaving it on in production.

[2026-04-20] - Vendor buy/sell pipeline, CharDef hash kimligi, isim pluralizasyonu, log ve tick optimizasyonlari
----------------------------------------

YENI OZELLIKLER / NEW FEATURES:
  - Vendor buy/sell akisi tamamlandi. Stok dedicated bir
    LAYER_VENDOR_STOCK (0x1A) konteynerinde tutuluyor, LAYER_VENDOR_EXTRA
    (0x1B) bos placeholder olarak donatiliyor. Buy menusu 0x2E (worn item)
    + 0x3C (container contents) + 0x74 (buy list) + 0x24 (open container)
    sirasinda gonderiliyor; 0x74 paketi gercek stok konteynerinin serial'ini
    kullaniyor ve isim alani bos itemler icin nameLen=1+null yazip
    ClassicUO'nun tiledata fallback'ini tetikliyor. Yeni 0x3C
    PacketContainerContents struct'i eklendi (gridIndex destekli).
  - VENDOR_S_* / VENDOR_B_* template'lerindeki SELL= / BUY= satirlari
    DefinitionLoader tarafindan parse ediliyor; "{lo hi}" dice araliginin
    ust degeri restock miktari olarak aliniyor.
  - SpeechEngine.OnPlayerSpeech eventi: oyuncu konusmasi NPC dispatch'inden
    once region seviyesinde tek seferlik tetikleniyor (guards / help guards
    gibi global keyword'ler icin).
  - CHARDEF parser "NPC=brain_vendor" ve "NPCBRAIN=Vendor" formlarinin
    ikisini de kabul ediyor; "brain_" / "npc_" onekleri otomatik temizleniyor.
  - LogFileLevel ayari iki sozdizimi destekliyor: tek deger (minimum esik)
    veya pipe/virgul ile beyaz liste ("Verbose | Warning | Error | Fatal").
    Whitelist modu Serilog sub-logger + Filter.ByIncludingOnly ile sarildi,
    konsol cikti seviyesi etkilenmiyor.

DUZELTMELER / FIXES:
  - Item display ID resolution: TemplateEngine.ResolveItemDefIndex (32-bit
    resource hash) ve ResolveDispId (16-bit wire grafigi) olarak ayrildi.
    String-hash'li ITEMDEF index'lerinin (>0xFFFF) ushort cast'lenip
    rastgele tile'a (lava / window-shutter / elven-plate) donusmesi
    engellendi. ItemDef.DispIndex / DupItemId zinciri hala onceleniyor.
  - ItemDef.Pluralize statik metodu eklendi (CItemBase::GetNamePluralize
    paritesi). Item.GetName() override'i %plural/singular% sablonlarini
    Amount'a gore runtime'da cozuyor — vendor listesi, click-name,
    tooltip ve crafting menulerinde "Black Pearl%s%" ham sablonu artik
    gorulmuyor (Corpse turu istisna, Source-X davranisi).
  - Character.CharDefIndex (24-bit defname hash) eklendi ve
    SpawnComponent / WorldSaver / WorldLoader (CHARDEFINDEX= property)
    tarafindan korunuyor. TriggerDispatcher, SpeechEngine.CommandHandler
    ve InfoSkillExtensions artik CharDef lookup'larinda BaseId yerine
    CharDefIndex kullaniyor — c_alchemist gibi string-named NPC'lerin
    body id'sine clamp edilip yanlis brain ile spawn olmasi giderildi.
  - GameWorld.FindRegion en kucuk toplam alanli region'u seciyor
    (CSector::GetRegion paritesi). AREADEF overlap'lerinde dis bolge
    icteki landmark'i (kale, sehir, dungeon) maskeliyor olmasi giderildi.
    OnRegionChanged hook'u CURRENT_REGION / CURRENT_REGION_UID tag'lerini
    de guncelliyor; FindAllRegions diagnostik helper eklendi.
  - DefinitionLoader.LoadCharDef ON=@ trigger headerlarinin ardindaki
    body satirlarini static CharDef state'ine bulastirmiyor — trigger
    govdesindeki NPC=... gibi atamalar artik CharDef template'ini degil,
    @Create runtime'inda Character instance'ini etkiliyor.
  - SpawnComponent NPC olusturduktan sonra OnNpcSpawned hook'unu firing
    ediyor; .add ile esdeger trigger zinciri (@Create -> brain finalisation
    -> @NPCRestock -> @CreateLoot) calisiyor. CharDefIndex spawn aninda
    set ediliyor.
  - WorldSaver/WorldLoader: CHARDEFINDEX kalici hale getirildi. Server
    restart sonrasinda c_alchemist / c_man brain hijack'i yeniden olusmuyor.

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - Multicore tick compute fazi: NpcDecision listesi ve ClientViewDelta
    dictionary'si static reusable buffer'lara cevrildi (per-tick gen-0 GC
    basincini dusurur).
  - ParallelComputeMinBatch=16 esigi: NPC veya client sayisi bu degerin
    altindaysa Parallel.ForEach yerine sequential foreach calisiyor;
    1-vCPU VDS host'larinda gozlemlenen 50-300 ms'lik thread pool ramp-up
    spike'lari ortadan kalkiyor.
  - Sub-loglama yapisi konsol sink'ini bloklamadan dosya filtresini
    bagimsiz uyguluyor; rutin INF mesajlari (komut/script/baglanti)
    artik logs/spherenet-*.log dosyasina yazilmiyor.

NEW FEATURES (EN):
  - Vendor buy/sell pipeline complete. Stock lives on a dedicated
    LAYER_VENDOR_STOCK (0x1A) container with an empty LAYER_VENDOR_EXTRA
    (0x1B) placeholder. Buy menu now sends 0x2E + 0x3C + 0x74 + 0x24 in
    order using the real stock container serial; empty item names emit
    nameLen=1+null so ClassicUO falls back to tiledata names. New
    PacketContainerContents (0x3C) writer added with grid-index support.
  - Vendor SELL= / BUY= rows in VENDOR_S_* / VENDOR_B_* templates are
    parsed; the upper bound of the "{lo hi}" dice range becomes the
    restock amount.
  - SpeechEngine.OnPlayerSpeech fires once per player utterance before
    per-NPC dispatch — used for region-level keywords (guards / help guards).
  - CHARDEF parser accepts both "NPC=brain_vendor" and "NPCBRAIN=Vendor",
    stripping "brain_" / "npc_" prefixes automatically.
  - LogFileLevel supports two syntaxes: single value (minimum threshold)
    or pipe/comma whitelist ("Verbose | Warning | Error | Fatal"). The
    whitelist mode is wired through a Serilog sub-logger +
    Filter.ByIncludingOnly so the console sink is unaffected.

FIXES (EN):
  - Item display ID resolution split into ResolveItemDefIndex (32-bit
    resource hash) and ResolveDispId (16-bit wire graphic). String-hashed
    ITEMDEF indices (>0xFFFF) no longer truncate via ushort cast into
    random tiles (lava / window-shutter / elven-plate). DispIndex /
    DupItemId chain still wins.
  - ItemDef.Pluralize + Item.GetName() override resolve %plural/singular%
    NAME= templates at read time using Amount. Vendor list, click-name,
    tooltip and crafting menus no longer leak raw "Black Pearl%s%"
    markers. Corpses skip pluralization to match Source-X.
  - Character.CharDefIndex (24-bit defname hash) added and persisted via
    SpawnComponent / WorldSaver / WorldLoader (CHARDEFINDEX=).
    TriggerDispatcher, SpeechEngine.CommandHandler and
    InfoSkillExtensions resolve CharDef via CharDefIndex instead of
    BaseId, fixing brain hijacks where string-named NPCs (c_alchemist,
    etc.) clamped to their body id and spawned with the wrong brain.
  - GameWorld.FindRegion now returns the smallest-total-area region
    matching the point (CSector::GetRegion parity). Overlapping AREADEFs
    no longer mask nested landmarks (castle / city / dungeon).
    OnRegionChanged also refreshes CURRENT_REGION / CURRENT_REGION_UID
    tags; FindAllRegions diagnostic helper added.
  - DefinitionLoader.LoadCharDef stops parsing keys after the first
    ON=@ trigger header so trigger-body assignments (NPC=, etc.) no
    longer pollute the static CharDef state — they apply to the
    Character instance at @Create time instead.
  - SpawnComponent invokes OnNpcSpawned after spawning so spawn-point
    NPCs receive the same trigger sequence as .add (@Create -> brain
    finalisation -> @NPCRestock -> @CreateLoot). CharDefIndex is set on
    spawn.
  - WorldSaver/WorldLoader persist CHARDEFINDEX. Restart no longer
    re-introduces c_alchemist / c_man brain hijacks.

PERFORMANCE (EN):
  - Multicore tick compute phase reuses static buffers for NpcDecision
    list and ClientViewDelta dictionary, lowering per-tick gen-0 GC
    pressure.
  - ParallelComputeMinBatch=16: when NPC or client count is below the
    threshold, sequential foreach replaces Parallel.ForEach. Eliminates
    50-300 ms thread-pool ramp-up spikes observed on 1-vCPU VDS hosts.
  - File sink runs through a sub-logger so console verbosity stays
    untouched; routine INF messages (commands / script loads /
    connections) no longer reach logs/spherenet-*.log.

    arrows/bolts in backpack -> COMBAT_ARCH_NOAMMO; swing aborted in both.
  - GameClient.HandleAttack: emits COMBAT_ATTACKS attacker emote on hit and
    COMBAT_MISSS sys message on a missed swing.
  - GameClient: added HasAmmoInBackpack helper that maps Bow -> Arrow and
    XBow -> Bolt before allowing the swing.
  - SpellEngine: new OnSysMessage callback wired up by Program.cs to deliver
    spell-specific text to the recipient client (Source-X
    CClientMsg::SysMessage parity).
  - SpellEngine.ApplySpecificSpell: Recall on an unmarked rune emits
    SPELL_RECALL_BLANK; Mark emits SPELL_MARK_CONT on success; GateTravel
    refuses unmarked runes and emits SPELL_GATE_OPEN otherwise; Poison spell
    posts the matching SPELL_POISON_<level> string to the victim.

[2026-04-20] - UUID sistemi, eski save otomatik migrasyon
----------------------------------------

YENI OZELLIKLER / NEW FEATURES:
  - Tum objelere (item + karakter) UUID (v7, zaman-sirali) ataniyor.
    Mevcut 32-bit Serial (UO protokolu icin) korunuyor, UUID ek tanimlayici
    olarak calisiyor. Save dosyasinda UUID= property olarak yaziliyor.
    Eski save dosyalari yuklendiginde UUID olmayan objeler icin otomatik
    UUID olusturuluyor — bir sonraki save'de kalici olarak yazilir.
    Script'ten <UUID> ile erisilebilir. GameWorld.FindByUuid() ile lookup.
    (UUID v7 (time-sortable) assigned to all objects (items + characters).
    Existing 32-bit Serial preserved for UO protocol. UUID written as
    UUID= property in save files. Old saves without UUID get auto-generated
    UUIDs on load — persisted on next save. Accessible via <UUID> in scripts.
    GameWorld.FindByUuid() for lookup.)

[2026-04-20] - ToolTipMode=0 single-click fix
----------------------------------------

DUZELTMELER / FIXES:
  - ToolTipMode=0 oldugunda tek tiklama (single click) calismiyordu. Neden:
    PacketCharList (0xA9) char list flags'te 0x20 (CLF_PALADIN_NECROMANCER_TOOLTIPS)
    her zaman acikti. ClassicUO bu flag'i gorunce TooltipsEnabled=true yapip tek
    tikta 0x09 SingleClick yerine 0xD6 tooltip request gonderiyor. Server
    ToolTipMode=0'da 0xD6'yi yutuyordu — click tamamen sessiz kaliyordu.
    Artik ToolTipMode=0'da char list flags'ten 0x20 bit'i kaldiriliyor, client
    klasik 0x09 SingleClick paketi gonderiyor.
    (ToolTipMode=0 single-click was silent. Root cause: PacketCharList (0xA9) always
    sent 0x20 in char list flags. ClassicUO sets TooltipsEnabled=true on that bit and
    sends 0xD6 tooltip requests instead of 0x09 SingleClick. Server dropped 0xD6 when
    ToolTipMode=0, making clicks appear dead. Now the 0x20 bit is stripped from char
    list flags when ToolTipMode=0, so the client sends classic 0x09 SingleClick.)

[2026-04-20] - Multi-DB connections, ToolTipMode, ClearCTags fix, GC optimizations
----------------------------------------

YENI OZELLIKLER / NEW FEATURES:
  - Coklu veritabani baglanti destegi: [MYSQL name] INI section'lari ile birden
    fazla veritabanina ayni anda baglanma. Her baglanti icin KeepAlive, timeout
    (connect/read/write), AutoConnect, UseThread (ayri is parcacigi) ayarlari.
    Eski tek-baglanti MySQL ayarlari (MySQLHost/MySQLUser/...) otomatik olarak
    "default" baglantiya donusturulur (backward compat).
    (Multi-database connection support: [MYSQL name] INI sections allow simultaneous
    connections to multiple databases. Per-connection KeepAlive, timeouts
    (connect/read/write), AutoConnect, UseThread settings. Legacy single-connection
    MySQL* keys auto-map to a "default" connection for backward compatibility.)

  - Yeni script komutlari: DB.CONNECT <name>, DB.SELECT <name>, DB.CLOSE <name>,
    DB.CLOSE *, <DB.CONNECTED.name>, <DB.ACTIVE>

    DB.CLOSE *, <DB.CONNECTED.name>, <DB.ACTIVE>)

    Config'den okunur, runtime'da GameWorld.ToolTipMode uzerinden kullanilir.

    Read from config, used at runtime via GameWorld.ToolTipMode.)

    buttonId==0 early return. ON=0 handlers like ClearCTags now execute, fixing

PERFORMANS / PERFORMANCE:
  - Sector.GetObjectsInRange: ToArray() kaldirildi, index-tabanli ters iterasyon
    ile sifir alokasyon. Multicore compute fazinda guvenli.
    (Sector.GetObjectsInRange: removed ToArray(), zero-allocation index-based
    reverse iteration. Safe during multicore compute phase.)

  - Program.cs: Reusable client snapshot listesi — her tick yeni List<> olusturmak
    yerine Clear() + yeniden doldurma. LINQ OrderBy yerine Array.Sort.
    (Reusable client snapshot list — Clear() + refill instead of new List<> per tick.
    Array.Sort replaces LINQ OrderBy for NPC decisions.)

  - GameWorld: Reusable _tickSectors/_tickSectorsSeen koleksiyonlari.
    ConsumeDirtyObjects() sifir alokasyonlu dirty-set drain methodu.
    (Reusable _tickSectors/_tickSectorsSeen collections.
    ConsumeDirtyObjects() zero-allocation dirty-set drain method.)

  - WorldLoader/StressTestEngine: DrainDirtyObjects -> ConsumeDirtyObjects guncellendi.
    (Updated DrainDirtyObjects -> ConsumeDirtyObjects across all call sites.)

[2026-04-20] - Item drop fix, Unicode speech, CHARDEF features, Sentry, name tracking
----------------------------------------

DUZELTMELER / FIXES:
  - 0x08 Drop paketi: post-6.0.1.7 client grid index byte'i atlanmiyordu,
    container serial 1 byte kayiyordu — item cantaya dusmuyordu, yere
    dusuyordu. Artik IsClientPost6017 kontroluyle grid index okunuyor.
    (Drop packet 0x08: grid index byte was not skipped for post-6.0.1.7
    clients, causing container serial to be read shifted by 1 byte —
    items fell to ground instead of container. Fixed with IsClientPost6017 check.)

  - Tum speech cikislari ASCII (0x1C) yerine Unicode (0xAE) kullanacak
    sekilde guncellendi. Turkce karakterler (s, c, g, i, o, u) artik
    dogru gorunuyor: player konusmasi, NPC speech, single-click label,
    MESSAGE ve SAYUA komutlari.
    (All speech output switched from ASCII PacketSpeechOut (0x1C) to Unicode
    PacketSpeechUnicodeOut (0xAE). Turkish characters now display correctly
    in player speech, NPC speech, labels, MESSAGE and SAYUA commands.)

  - .add komutu: hedef container/karakter secildiginde item artik cantaya
    dusuyor (PlaceAddedItem akisi). Onceden her zaman yere dusuyordu.
    (.add command: when targeting a container or character, item now goes
    into the pack via PlaceAddedItem flow instead of always dropping to ground.)

  - ContainedIn dogrudan atama yerine AddItem() kullaniliyor: GatheringEngine,
    SkillHandlers, TradeEngine, vendor restock, NPC equip. Container _contents
    listesi artik tutarli.
    (Replaced direct ContainedIn assignment with AddItem() across gathering,
    skills, trade, vendor restock, and NPC equip — container contents list
    now stays consistent.)

  - Drop trigger reject (DropOn_Item/Self/Char) durumunda item kaybolmuyordu
    ama PlaceItemInPack ile cantaya bounce ediliyor artik.
    (Drop trigger rejection now bounces item back to pack via PlaceItemInPack
    instead of silently losing it.)

  - ExpressionParser: DEF./DEF0. ile baslayan degiskenler artik 'D' prefix
    (decimal force) olarak yanlis yorumlanmiyor.
    (ExpressionParser: DEF./DEF0. prefixed variables no longer misinterpreted
    as decimal-force 'D' prefix.)

YENI OZELLIKLER / NEW FEATURES:
  - CHARDEF skill adi ile property atama: MAGICRESISTANCE, TACTICS vb. skill
    isimleri artik dogrudan CHARDEF'te ve script property olarak kullanilabiliyor.
    Alternatif isimler destekleniyor (RESISTINGSPELLS, EVALINT, DETECTHIDDEN vb.).
    (Skill name-based property assignment: MAGICRESISTANCE, TACTICS etc. can be
    used directly in CHARDEF and script properties. Alternate names supported.)

  - @CreateLoot trigger: @Create'den sonra ateslenip loot spawn icin kullaniliyor.
    (@CreateLoot trigger: fires after @Create for loot spawning.)

    CHARDEF'te ve runtime'da destekleniyor. CombatEngine elemental split ile

  - CHARDEF: SUBSECTION, DESCRIPTION, FOLLOWERSLOTS property'leri eklendi.
    (CHARDEF: added SUBSECTION, DESCRIPTION, FOLLOWERSLOTS properties.)

  - Karakter isim degisiklik takibi: Name setter ve TrySetProperty("NAME")

[2026-04-19] - Vendor ciplak fix v3: Layer'i tiledata.mul Quality byte'indan resolve
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  v2'de item'lar spawn ediliyordu ama still hala ciplak kaliyordu.
  Sebep: sphere scriptlerinde ITEMDEF'lerin LAYER= satirlari
  yorumlu ("//LAYER=layer_shirt"). ItemDef.Layer = None ile
  SpawnAndEquipItem backpack'e atiyordu — 0x78 equipment list'te
  sadece 0E 75 (backpack) goruluyor.

  Source-X Wearable-flag'li tile'larin Quality byte'ini layer indexi
  olarak kullaniyor (tiledata.mul). SpawnAndEquipItem ve
  EquipNewbieItems artik Layer.None durumunda GameWorld.MapData
  uzerinden GetItemTileData okuyup TileFlag.Wearable ve Quality'e
  bakiyor. Boylece i_shirt_plain layer=Shirt, i_pants_short
  layer=Pants, i_boots_calf layer=Shoes olarak equip ediliyor.

  v2 spawned items but the NPC still looked naked. Cause: the
  Sphere-format ITEMDEFs have their LAYER= line commented out
  ("//LAYER=layer_shirt"). With ItemDef.Layer = None,
  SpawnAndEquipItem dropped each item into the backpack — the
  0x78 equipment list only showed 0E 75 (backpack).

  Source-X reads the layer from tiledata.mul: items with the
  Wearable flag store their layer index in the Quality byte.
  SpawnAndEquipItem and EquipNewbieItems now fall back to
  GameWorld.MapData.GetItemTileData when ItemDef.Layer is None,
  check TileFlag.Wearable, and use Quality as the layer. Shirts,
  pants, boots, hats etc. now equip correctly.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - Character.SpawnAndEquipItem: Layer.None fallback
    ResolveTileDataLayer helper'ina.
  - Character.ResolveTileDataLayer (yeni): Wearable flag kontrolu +
    Quality -> Layer cast.
  - GameClient.EquipNewbieItems: ayni tiledata fallback'i (iki
    path da tutarli kalsin diye).

TEST:
  - .add c_alchemist: 0x78 equipment list'te sirt + pantolon +
    ayakkabi + sapka + robe + dagger + backpack'in hepsi layer'lari
    ile goruluyor olmali. .info ile paperdoll EquippedItems
    listesi dolu olmali.

================================================================================

[2026-04-19] - Vendor ciplak fix v2: @Create trigger body + DEFNAME pool
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Onceki commit'te NPC hala ciplak geliyordu. Iki ayri neden:

  1) Script'te ITEM=/COLOR= satirlari ROOT CHARDEF level'da degil,
     ON=@Create trigger body'sinde. CharDef loader @Create'i atliyor
     (trigger runner'a birakiyor) — NewbieItems listesi bos kaliyor.
     Dolayisiyla EquipNewbieItems hicbir sey yapmiyordu.

  2) random_shirts_human / random_hats / random_male_hair gibi
     "template" isimleri aslinda [TEMPLATE] bloklari degil —
     [DEFNAME items_clothing] bloklari icindeki weighted-list
     entry'leri: "random_shirts_human { i_shirt_plain 1 ... }".
     TemplateEngine sadece TemplateDef ariyordu, defname tablo
     bosunu gormuyordu.

  Iki dugum ayni anda kapatildi.

  The previous commit still left NPCs naked. Two causes:

  1) The ITEM=/COLOR= lines live inside the @Create trigger body,
     not at the CHARDEF root — the CharDef loader intentionally
     skips @Create (leaves it to the trigger runner), so the
     NewbieItems list was always empty and EquipNewbieItems
     ran with nothing to do.

  2) random_shirts_human / random_hats / random_male_hair etc.
     are not [TEMPLATE] blocks. They live as weighted-list entries
     inside [DEFNAME items_clothing]: "random_shirts_human
     { i_shirt_plain 1 i_shirt_fancy 1 ... }". TemplateEngine only
     looked up TemplateDef and never consulted the defname text
     table, so every random_* resolved to nothing.

  Both paths are fixed now.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - Character.TryExecuteCommand: ITEM=, ITEMNEWBIE=, COLOR= verb'leri
    eklendi. ITEM= random_* pool resolve eder, item spawn eder,
    NPC'ye equip (layer'a) veya backpack'e koyar. COLOR= en son
    spawn edilen item'in hue'sunu ayarlar (match_* onceki hue'yu
    kullanir). Verb sirasi @Create trigger body'sinde sahip oldugu
    anlami tasir.
  - Character.SpawnAndEquipItem / ResolveColorArg / RollDice
    helper'lari.
  - TemplateEngine.PickRandomItemDefName: artik
    ResourceHolder.TryGetDefValue'ya dusuyor. "{ a w b w ... }"
    weighted string'ini parse edip weight'e gore rastgele entry
    secer; tek alias formunu (random_footwear_elven i_elven_boots)
    da destekler.
  - TemplateEngine.PickFromDefValue (yeni helper).

TEST:
  - .add c_alchemist -> robe, pantolon, ayakkabi, sapka, dagger ile
    gelmeli; hair/beard colors_hair renginde; robe colors_red.
  - .info <npc> -> Inspect dialog'da EquippedItems listesi dolu.

     resolves template defnames to a random itemdef. COLOR=

  3) Vendor NPCs fire @NPCRestock on creation. Character gets new

[2026-04-19] - Banker / Vendor / Healer NPC keyword dispatch (legacy save uyumluluk)
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Legacy Sphere save'leri banker/vendor/healer NPC'lerini NPC_HUMAN
  brain ile kaydediyor; gerçek davranış TSPEECH script bloklariyla
  sağlanıyordu. O bloklar bu shard'da tanımlı olmayınca servisçi
  NPC'ler "bank" / "buy" / "heal" keyword'lerine sessiz kaliyordu.
  Iki duzeltme:

  1) TryParseNpcBrain artik "NPC_HUMAN", "NPC_BANKER" gibi Source-X
     save token'larini enum'a mappliyor (onceden None donuyordu).
  2) OnNpcHearSpeech icinde brain Human/None ise NPC adina bakip
     "banker", "healer", "stable", "guard", "vendor"/"merchant"
     kelimesi gecerse o brain'in davranis kolunu calistiriyor.
     Bu sayede legacy save'deki "Brian the Banker" isimli Human
     brain NPC de "bank" deyince bank box aciyor.

  Legacy Sphere saves register banker/vendor/healer NPCs with the
  NPC_HUMAN brain and leave the real behaviour to TSPEECH script
  blocks. When those blocks aren't loaded on this shard the service
  NPC stays mute for "bank" / "buy" / "heal". Two fixes:

  1) TryParseNpcBrain now accepts Source-X save tokens like
     "NPC_HUMAN" / "NPC_BANKER" (previously these fell through to
     None).
  2) OnNpcHearSpeech inspects the NPC name when brain is Human/None
     and routes to banker/healer/stable/guard/vendor behaviour when
     the name contains that role keyword. A legacy "Brian the
     Banker" human-brain NPC now responds to "bank" by opening the
     speaker's bank box.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - Character.cs: TryParseNpcBrain NPC_/BRAIN_ onekini siyriyor.
  - Program.cs: OnNpcHearSpeech inferredBrain mantigi, switch
    inferredBrain uzerinde. Human-isim-bazli fallback.
