[2026-04-19] - Notoriety: overhead name hue (single-click label) artik noto rengi
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Mouse-hover veya auto-label ile tetiklenen overhead isim
  paketinde (0x1C) hue hardcoded 0x03B2 (gri) idi — noto byte
  (0x77/0x78'de) dogru olsa bile istemci "You see: Name" etiketini
  sabit gri cikariyordu. HandleSingleClick icinde Character hedefi
  icin hue artik NotoToHue(GetNotoriety(ch)) ile hesaplaniyor.
  Source-X CServerConfig m_iColorNoto* sabitleri kullanildi:
  blue=0x59, green=0x3F, grey=0x3B2, orange=0x90, red=0x22,
  yellow=0x35.

  The overhead label packet (0x1C) that fires on mouse-hover /
  auto-label had a hardcoded hue of 0x03B2 (grey) — so even with a
  correct noto byte in 0x77/0x78, the "You see: Name" line always
  came up grey. HandleSingleClick now picks the hue via
  NotoToHue(GetNotoriety(ch)) for character targets. Values follow
  Source-X CServerConfig m_iColorNoto* defaults: blue=0x59,
  green=0x3F, grey=0x3B2, orange=0x90, red=0x22, yellow=0x35.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - GameClient.HandleSingleClick: Character targets artik noto'ya
    gore hue kullaniyor; Item target'lari 0x03B2 gri kaliyor.
  - GameClient.NotoToHue: yeni static helper — byte 1..7 → hue.

ETKI / IMPACT:
  - Mouse-hover / tek tiklama ile Oyuncu mavi, PK kirmizi,
    criminal gri, enemy guild turuncu, party/ally yesil,
    invul sari goruluyor.

[2026-04-19] - Notoriety: NPC brain/karma bazli renk
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:

  mantigi uygulaniyor:
  - monster/berserk/dragon → 6 (kirmizi)
  - healer/banker → 7 (sari, invul by role)
  - guard/vendor/stable/human → 1 (mavi, friendly)
  - animal → 3 (gri, wild)
  - karma ≤ -2000 → 6 (kirmizi), karma ≤ -500 → 4 (gri criminal),
    karma > 500 (None brain) → 1 (mavi)

  GetNotoriety no longer returns blanket 3 (grey) for NPCs — now
  dispatches on brain type and karma like Source-X Noto_CalcFlag:
  - monster/berserk/dragon → 6 (red)
  - healer/banker → 7 (yellow, invul by role)
  - guard/vendor/stable/human → 1 (blue, friendly)
  - animal → 3 (grey, wild)
  - karma ≤ -2000 → 6 (red), karma ≤ -500 → 4 (grey criminal),
    karma > 500 (None brain) → 1 (blue)

[2026-04-19] - Notoriety: legacy save IsPlayer flag + ACCOUNT-tag fallback
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Legacy Sphere save dosyalari ISPLAYER bayragini yazmiyor. Bu
  durumda yuklenen player karakterler IsPlayer=false ile geliyor
  ve GetNotoriety onlari NPC sayip gri dondurinyor. Iki yerli fix:

  1) WorldLoader artik account linkage sirasinda ch.IsPlayer=true
     set ediyor — ACCOUNT tag'i varsa onun oyuncu oldugu kesin.
  2) GetNotoriety defensive fallback: IsPlayer=false ama ACCOUNT
     tag'i varsa yine player gibi degerlendiriliyor. Boylece
     restart beklemeden mevcut calisan shard'larda da duzelir.

  Legacy Sphere saves don't write the ISPLAYER flag, so imported
  player characters load with IsPlayer=false and GetNotoriety
  classifies them as NPCs (grey). Two fixes:

  1) WorldLoader now sets ch.IsPlayer=true during account linking —
     a linked ACCOUNT tag is authoritative proof of player status.
  2) GetNotoriety defensive fallback: when IsPlayer=false but the
     ACCOUNT tag is set, still treat as player. This covers shards
     already running off a pre-fix world file without needing a
     restart.

[2026-04-19] - Notoriety + combat animation + swing sound
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  War modunda overhead isim renkleri sadece gri cikiyordu ve
  saldirilar bogazi yokken yay sesi uretiyordu. Uc degisiklik:

  1) GetNotoriety Source-X NOTO_TYPE tablosuna gore 1-7 doner —
     innocent=mavi, friend/party/guild-ally=yesil, NPC=gri,
     criminal=gri-flagged, enemy-guild=turuncu, murderer=kirmizi,
     invulnerable=sari.
  2) Saldiri animasyonu artik PacketAnimation (0x6E) kullaniyor —
     eski PacketEffect (0x70) grafik=0 ile "gorunmez mermi"
     olarak davraniyor ve client arrow sesi calistiyordu.
  3) Yeni GetSwingSound — silah tipine gore swing baslangic sesi
     ayrilmis (bow=draw, blade=whoosh, mace=bash, unarmed=whoosh).
     Eski kodda yalnizca hit-land sesi vardi.

  Overhead name hues in war mode were stuck on grey, and unarmed
  attacks produced a phantom bow sound. Three fixes:

  1) GetNotoriety now returns Source-X NOTO_TYPE 1-7 —
     innocent/blue, friend/green, NPC-neutral/grey, criminal/grey,
     enemy-guild/orange, murderer/red, invulnerable/yellow.
  2) Swing animation uses PacketAnimation (0x6E) instead of
     PacketEffect (0x70) with graphic=0, which the client was
     rendering as an invisible projectile (the source of the bow
     sound).
  3) New GetSwingSound picks a weapon-appropriate swing-start
     tone (bow draw, blade whoosh, mace bash, unarmed whoosh).
     Previously only the hit-land sound played.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - GameClient.GetNotoriety: tam Source-X mapping (invul, murderer,
    criminal, guild war/ally, party, NPC, innocent default).
    ResolveGuildManager / ResolvePartyFinder delegate'leri kullanir.
  - GameClient.HandleAttack: PacketEffect yerine PacketAnimation
    (0x6E) ile swing anim; yeni GetSwingAction silaha gore 0x6E
    action index'ini seciyor (bow=18, xbow=19, sword/axe=9,
    fence=13, mace=11, throwing=12, unarmed=31).
  - GameClient.GetSwingSound: silah tipine gore swing sesi.
  - Hit-land sound conserved (ayri PacketSound, target konumunda).

ETKI / IMPACT:
  - War mode'da saldirdigimiz karakterin rengi artik notoriety'ye
    gore doğru gozukuyor.
  - Varsayilan player player'a mavi (innocent) goruluyor; NPC gri;
    parti/guild arkadasi yesil.
  - Saldiri animasyonu artik swing olarak cikiyor; silahsiz
    saldirida yay sesi gelmez.

[2026-04-19] - Fix: GO / src.p teleport sektor transfer + out-of-bounds guard
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Character.MoveTo ve ObjBase TrySetProperty("P") artik sadece
  Position alanini degil, dunya sektor indexini de guncelliyor.
  Onceki sektor-bazli broadcast fix'i bu eksik davranisi gorunur

  atiyor, karakter eski konumunda kaliyor.

  Character.MoveTo and ObjBase TrySetProperty("P") now update the
  world's sector index, not just the Position field. The earlier
  sector-based broadcast fix exposed this gap (the old
  _clients.Values scan used to reach stranded characters anyway).
  GameWorld.MoveCharacter and PlaceCharacter now refuse moves to
  a null sector (out-of-bounds / unknown map) with a warning log;
  the character stays at its previous location.

    world.MoveCharacter cagiriyor; world resolve edilemezse
    eski Position = target fallback'i.

    Item icin PlaceItem cagiriyor; diger objeler icin duz
    _position atamasi.
  - GameWorld.cs: MoveCharacter/PlaceCharacter null sektor
    durumunda early return + _logger.LogWarning; karakter eski
    sektorunde kalir.

ETKI / IMPACT:
  - .GO 9999,9999 gibi out-of-bounds komutlar artik karakteri
    "sessiz kaybetmez". Yayin (broadcast) gorunurlugu korunur.
  - Tum MoveCharacter yollarindaki out-of-bounds koruma ortak.

[2026-04-19] - Perf: multicore default on + WeatherEngine + BroadcastNearby sektor index
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Busy shard hedefi (500 online / 1M item / 300k char) icin uc tick
  darbogazi kapatildi:
  1) MulticoreEnabled default'u true yapildi — paralel sektor tick'i
     devreye girdi (fallback exception path zaten mevcuttu).

     BroadcastCharacterAppear 500-player lineer _clients taramasi
     yerine 3x3 sektor penceresi + char-UID -> client sozlugu kullaniyor.

  Closed three tick bottlenecks for busy-shard scale:
  1) MulticoreEnabled now defaults to true — the parallel sector tick
     runs in practice (the fallback exception path stays as before).
  2) WeatherEngine.OnTick visits only regions that contain an online
     player, skipping the full _world.Regions scan.
  3) BroadcastNearby / BroadcastMoveNearby / SendPacketToChar /
     BroadcastCharacterAppear use a char-UID -> client dict plus a
     3x3 sector window instead of linearly scanning _clients.

  - WeatherEngine.cs: OnTick aktif sektor region'lari uzerinden

    eklendi — diger sistemler dis alana iterate edebiliyor.

    Action delegate'leri; HandleLoginComplete ve OnDisconnect icinde
    tetikleniyor.
  - Program.cs: _clientsByCharUid sozlugu; GameClient delegate'leri
    aracligiyla bakimi. BroadcastNearby/MoveNearby sektor penceresi
    (range/sectorsize+1 yari capli) + sozluk lookup. SendPacketToChar
    direk sozluk lookup (O(N) -> O(1)). BroadcastCharacterAppear
    ayni sektor pencereli mantik.

ETKI / IMPACT:
  - 500 online, 1M item, 300k char senaryosunda beklenen:
    tick ortalamasi ~100-200ms -> ~30-60ms; peak ~500ms -> ~150-200ms.
    Ping dalgalanmasi belirgin sekilde azalir.
  - Davranis degisikligi yok — broadcast mesafe kontrolu aynen
    korundu, sadece filtre erken uygulaniyor.

[2026-04-19] - Corpse decay: TAG yerine per-item timer (slow_tick fix)
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Corpse decay artik Item.DecayTime field'ina yaziliyor; sektor-uyku
  tick yolu (Item.OnTick) icinden dusuyor. Eski DeathEngine.ProcessDecay
  her tick'te tum dunyadaki item'lari taraip DECAY_TIME TAG'ini
  okuyordu — bu flush fazinda ~100 ms harciyordu (slow_tick uyarisinin
  kaynagi). Source-X davranisiyla uyumlu: CItem::_SetTimeout + sector
  tick, merkezi scanner yok.

  Corpse decay now uses Item.DecayTime (driven by sector-aware
  Item.OnTick) rather than a DECAY_TIME tag. The old
  DeathEngine.ProcessDecay full-world scan that read that tag ran
  every tick and cost ~100 ms in the flush phase — the source of
  the observed slow_tick warnings. Matches Source-X: per-item
  CItem::_SetTimeout driven by the sector tick, no central scanner.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - DeathEngine.cs: corpse.SetTag("DECAY_TIME", ...) yerine
    corpse.DecayTime = ... kullaniliyor. ProcessDecay metodu
    tamamen kaldirildi.
  - Item.cs: OnTick decay dalinda ItemType.Corpse icin
    OnCorpseDecay static delegate'i cagriliyor (contents'i yere
    dusur). Mevcut spell-field / summoned-item decay pattern'i
    ile ayni.
  - Program.cs: Item.OnCorpseDecay delegate'i
    corpse.Contents -> _world.PlaceItem(child, corpse.Position)
    sekilde wire edildi. RunPostTickMaintenance'teki
    _deathEngine.ProcessDecay cagrisi kaldirildi.

ETKI / IMPACT:
  - Flush fazi artik dunyada kac item oldugundan bagimsiz — sabit
    birkac ms. Busy-world'de slow_tick gozleme sifirlanir.
  - Corpse decay zamanlamasi degismedi (NPC: CorpseNpcDecay dk,
    player: CorpsePlayerDecay dk).

[2026-04-19] - Dialog motor tamamlayici: DSRC, serv.allclients, '<' vs LT
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Dialog motoruna admin-tarzi script paketlerinin bagli oldugu
  birkac eksik parca eklendi: serv.allclients yineleyici, DSRC.
  prefix, ve kritik bir ExpressionParser hata duzeltmesi — "<"
  karakteri bracket aciklamasi mi yoksa less-than operatoru mu
  ayrimi simdi sonraki karaktere gore yapiliyor.

  Filled in the remaining gaps that admin-style script packs
  need: serv.allclients iterator, DSRC. prefix mirroring SRC.,
  and a critical ExpressionParser fix — '<' now disambiguates
  between bracket-open and less-than based on the following
  character.

SERV.ALLCLIENTS / SERV.ALLCLIENTS:
  - Script verb "Serv.AllClients <func>" (veya "AllClients <func>")
    artik online her karakter icin <func>'u cagiriyor; src
    caller olarak kaliyor. Protokol: _ALLCLIENTS=<srcUid>|<func>
    ServerPropertyResolver uzerinden Program.cs'nin
    HandleAllClients'ine yonleniyor.
  - Her iterasyon yeni TriggerArgs ile calisir: target=online
    character, Source=srcChar. Iteration oncesi _clients
    snapshot'i alinir ki callback CTag mutasyonlari iteration'u
    etkilemesin.
  / "serv.allclients <func>" now invokes <func> once per online
    player with the caller preserved as src. Snapshot-iteration
    so callback-side CTag mutations don't disturb the loop.

DSRC. PREFIX:
  - ScriptInterpreter.ResolveVarForTarget ve dialog expander
    resolver'lari hem SRC. hem DSRC. prefix'ini kabul ediyor.
    Storage ayni; DSRC. yalnizca Sphere konvansiyonunun
    "decimal-forced read" sinyalidir.
  / Accept DSRC. alongside SRC. — shared storage, signals
    numeric-context read. Fixes "<dSrc.CTag0.X>" lookups that
    were previously unresolved.

ANGLE-BRACKET vs LESS-THAN / ANGLE-BRACKET vs LESS-THAN:
  - ResolveAngleBrackets ve ReadAngleBracket "<" ile
    karsilastiginda bir sonraki karaktere bakiyor: identifier
    basi (harf veya '_') ise bracket acilisi, diger durumda
    (bosluk / rakam / '=' / paren) less-than operatoru.
  - Onceki davranis: script'in "<A> < <B>" ifadesinde ortadaki
    ' < ' LT operatorunu bracket acilisi saniyor, outer read
    EOF'a kadar yutuyordu. Ornek: admin_getplayers
    "If ((<Src.Account.Plevel> < <Account.Plevel>) ..." satiri
    tamamen mal formed oluyor ve IF koskulu cope donuyor,
    fonksiyon hic ilerlemiyordu.
  / '<' followed by a letter/'_' opens a bracket; anything else
    (space, digit, '=', paren) is treated as the less-than
    operator and passes through literally. Fixes expressions
    like "<A.X> < <B.Y>" that were misread as a single runaway
    bracket.

DIALOG BUTTON GORSEL SYNC / DIALOG BUTTON VISIBLE SYNC:
  - TryRunScriptDialogButton handler calistirmadan once
    Position, BodyId, Hue, StatFlags snapshot aliyor. Sonra
    pozisyon degistiyse world.MoveCharacter + Resync +
    BroadcastDrawObject; pozisyon sabit ama goruntuyu
    etkileyen alanlar degistiyse sadece BroadcastDrawObject.
  - Script'te "src.body=X" / "src.hue=Y" / "src.flags|=
    statf_hidden" gibi atamalar artik anlik gorsel effect
    yaratiyor; TrySetProperty private field'lari guncelliyor
    ama client'a bildirim gitmiyordu.
  / Snapshot body / hue / flags alongside position; broadcast
    DrawObject when any changed. src.body= / src.hue= /
    src.flags|= script assignments propagate to nearby clients
    without a full resync.

REFN / REFN.PROPERTY:
  - Dialog expander "REFn=<val>" atamalarini tanir (REF1..REFn,
    '.' icermez) ve resolved degeri locals sozlugunde "REFN"
    anahtariyla saklar. <REFn> stored degeri doner;
    <REFn.property> _REF_GET=<uid>|<prop> protokolune delege
    eder ve referans aldigi objenin ozellikleri dialog'a akar.
  / Scope-local object references for dialog expansion.
    <REFn> returns the stored value; <REFn.property> walks
    to the referenced object via _REF_GET.

CTAG / CTAG0 DIALOG OKUMASI / CTAG DIALOG READS:
  - <CTag.X> ve <CTag0.X> dialog expander'da karakterin
    gercek tag deposundan okunuyor; unset ise "0" doner
    (Sphere default).
  / <CTag.X> / <CTag0.X> now resolve to the character's
    stored tag in the dialog expander, not a fixed "0".

FALLBACK DELEGATION / FALLBACK DELEGATION:
  - ResolveInlineExpressions sonunda bilinmeyen varName'ler
    TryResolveScriptVariable'a delege ediliyor — ACCOUNT.X,
    ISEVENT.X, ISDIALOGOPEN.X, VAR0.X, GETREFTYPE, DEFMSG.X
    vb. dialog scope'ta ayni cevabi veriyor.
  / Unknown variable names fall through to
    TryResolveScriptVariable so ACCOUNT.x / VAR0.x /
    ISEVENT.x / DEFMSG.x resolve inside dialog expansion
    the same way they do at runtime.

      REF1=<SERV.ACCOUNT.<Eval <CTag0.Index>+1>>
      <REF1.NAME> / <REF1.PLEVEL> / <REF1.LASTIP>
  / REFn references stored in the dialog-local scope; <REFn>
    returns the raw value, <REFn.property> resolves via the
    existing _REF_GET protocol. Admin-style listing dialogs can
    now populate rows with account / character properties.

CTAG / CTAG0 OKUMA / CTAG READS:
  - <CTag.X> ve <CTag0.X> dialog expander'da karakterin
    gercek tag'ine bakiyor (Character.TryGetTag); bulunmazsa
    "0" Sphere varsayilani.
  - Onceki davranis: her CTag "0" donuyordu — admin dialog'lari
    page / search / counters'i CTag'te saklayamiyordu.
  / <CTag.X> / <CTag0.X> now read from the character's actual
    tag storage (default "0" when unset per Sphere convention).

ACCOUNT / FALLBACK DELEGATION:
  - ResolveInlineExpressions'in sonuna fallback:
    _character.TryResolveScriptVariable(varName, ...).
  - ACCOUNT.X, ISEVENT.X, ISDIALOGOPEN.X, VAR0.X, GETREFTYPE,
    DEFMSG.X gibi accessors artik dialog scope'ta ayni sonucu
    veriyor — onceden yalnizca script calistirma zamaninda
    cozuluyorlardi.
  / Fallback to TryResolveScriptVariable covers ACCOUNT.x,
    VAR0.x, ISEVENT.x, ISDIALOGOPEN.x, GETREFTYPE, DEFMSG.x —
    the same resolver runtime code uses. Dialog rendering now
    matches runtime resolution.

GORSEL STATE SYNC / VISIBLE STATE SYNC:
  - TryRunScriptDialogButton pre-execution snapshot:
    Position, BodyId, Hue, StatFlags.
  - Post-execution: pozisyon degistiyse world.MoveCharacter +
    Resync + BroadcastDrawObject (teleport yolu);
    degismediyse ama goruntusu degistiyse (body / hue /
    flags) sadece BroadcastDrawObject.
  - Script'te "src.body=X", "src.hue=Y", "src.flags|=
    statf_hidden" gibi atamalar artik anlik gorsel effect
    yaratiyor — onceden TrySetProperty private field'lari
    degistiriyor ama client'a bildirim gitmiyordu.
  / Snapshot body / hue / flags alongside position; broadcast
    DrawObject when any changed. src.body= / src.hue= /
    src.flags|= assignments propagate to nearby clients
    without needing an extra resync call.


[2026-04-19] - Dialog sistemi tamamlamasi + .add itemdef zincir cozumu
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Sphere dialog layout interpreter'i kontrol akisi komutlari (IF /
  FOR / WHILE / LOCAL), gelismis expression resolver'lar ve button
  handler altyapisiyla tamamlandi. 0xAD keyword-mode speech parser
  eklendi — modern ClassicUO'nun gonderdigi komutlar hicten silent
  drop edilmek yerine command dispatcher'a ulasiyor. Scripted
  itemdef'lerden (".add i_moongate" gibi) olusturulan esyalar
  trigger'larini koruyor.

  The Sphere dialog layout interpreter is now control-flow-aware
  (IF / FOR / WHILE / LOCAL) with richer expression resolution and a
  working button handler. 0xAD keyword-mode (type 0xC0) speech is
  parsed — modern ClassicUO commands reach the dispatcher instead of
  being silently dropped. Scripted itemdef creations ('.add ...')
  carry their triggers forward.

0xAD KEYWORD SPEECH / 0xAD KEYWORD SPEECH:
  - ClassicUO 7.0.20 kisilik keywordlu speech'i type 0xC0 ile
    gonderiyor. Eski handler sadece plain mode'u biliyordu;
    keyword block'unu text sanip UTF-16 BE olarak okuyor, komut
    metni bos geliyordu — butun ".command" girdileri sessizce
    dusurulmustu.
  - Yeni handler isEncoded=(type & 0xC0)!=0 ile ayirt ediyor;
    keyword listesini servuo bit-packed formatiyla skip edip
    text'i UTF-8 null-terminated olarak okuyor. Encoded flag
    temizleniyor ki speech routing plain-mode type'i gorsun.
  / UTF-8 text + keyword-list skip matching ServUO's
    UnicodeSpeech packet reader. Admin / script dialog commands
    typed while the client was in keyword mode now reach the
    dispatcher.

DIALOG LAYOUT KONTROL AKISI / DIALOG LAYOUT CONTROL FLOW:
  - ExpandDialogScriptKeys: layoutSection key listesini render
    switch'ine vermeden once pre-expand ediyor.
  - IF / ELSE / ELIF / ENDIF: kondisyon resolve edilip dogru dal
    seciliyor.
  - FOR N / FOR start end / ENDFOR: _for iteratoru ile unroll,
    max 500 iter.
  - WHILE cond / ENDWHILE: condition her iter'de yeniden
    degerlendirilir.
  - LOCAL.x = value / += / -= / |= / &= / ^= / .=: scope'lu
    local variable atamalari.
  / New layout pre-expander handles IF / FOR / WHILE / LOCAL
    blocks before commands reach the render switch. Loops unroll
    with the `_for` iterator; local scope flows into subsequent
    expression resolution.

EXPRESSION RESOLVER'LAR / EXPRESSION RESOLVERS:
  - ResolveInlineExpressions: dialog-local scope ile entegre
    resolver. Destekler:
      <LOCAL.x>, <DLOCAL.x>        — scope + uninitialized "0"
      <ARGN>, <ARGN1>              — dialog arg (page / sdialog arg)
      <DEF.x>, <DEF0.x>            — string + numeric tables
      <SRC.property>               — current character's property
      <SERV.property>              — server-level resolver
  - ScriptInterpreter.ResolveVarForTarget'e DLOCAL. eklendi; hem
    dialog layout'ta hem de button handler body'sinde ayni
    scope okunuyor.
  - DEF / DEF0 lookup: TryGetDefValue (_defTexts) basarisizsa
    ResolveDefName (_defNames, numeric) fallback; bulunmazsa
    "0" donuyor — Sphere semantigi.
  / Dialog-local scope, args-feed, DEF / DEF0 string+numeric
    lookup, uninitialised-zero fallback. Identical semantics

    ayrimi: paren-depth testi sadece depth==1 iken uygulaniyor

  - Onceki davranis: <eval 62+(<local._for>*25)> icinde ic '>'
    GT sanilip outer read EOF'a kadar yutuyordu.
  / ReadAngleBracket now only applies the paren-depth GT
    disambiguation at the outermost bracket. Nested <...>
    inside parens closes normally.

    dialog handler'larinin "args=<def0...>" + "<argv[N]>" akisi

    ("1828,2948,-20,0,Minoc" -> 5 token).
  - <ARGCHK> (bare): herhangi bir switch secili mi 1/0.
  - <ARGCHKID>: ilk seçili switch'in ID'si (yoksa 0).

  / Script-side args= now mutates TriggerArgs.ArgString; ARGV

    hem CollectDialogButtonBody delimiter.
  - TryRunScriptDialogButton postscript: script calistirmadan

  / ONBUTTON=N accepted as an ON=N alias. Dialog button
    handler now captures pre-execution position and

  - ScriptKey.Parse simdi |=, &=, ^= operatorlerini

[2026-04-19] - Variable-length paket length + 0xDF buff icon formati
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Variable-length paketlerde CreateVariable'dan sonra
  WriteLengthAt(1) cagrisi yoktu: length byte'lari placeholder 0
  olarak kaliyordu. 0xDF BuffIcon'u aldiginda ClassicUO paket
  parser state'i bozuluyor ve istemci hard-freeze oluyor. Ayrica
  0xDF'in icerik duzeni de ServUO AddBuffPacket formatiyla
  uyumsuzdu — kendi "title length + ham metin" yapimiz yerine
  cliloc + args formatini kullanmak gerekiyordu.

  Variable-length packets were missing their WriteLengthAt(1)
  call, so the length bytes stayed at the CreateVariable
  placeholder of 0. Receiving a 0xDF BuffIcon with length 0
  deadlocked ClassicUO's packet parser and hard-froze the client.
  The 0xDF body layout also diverged from ServUO's AddBuffPacket
  format (title length + raw text vs. title cliloc + args).

LENGTH BYTE FIX / LENGTH BYTE FIX:
  - PacketBuffIcon (0xDF) Build sonunda WriteLengthAt(1) yoktu —
    60-74 byte paket, gercekte length alani 0x0000.
  - 0xBF sub 0x06 party paketleri (MemberList, RemoveMember,
    Message, Invitation) hepsinde ayni eksik vardi. Party
    invite / member broadcast / chat hepsi client'ta donuyordu.
  / Added the missing WriteLengthAt(1) to five classes. Variable-
    length packets now report the real body size.

0xDF FORMATI / 0xDF FORMAT:
  - Eski: serial + iconId + add + source(4) + iconId + 1 +
    unk(4) + duration + unk(2) + unk(1) + titleLength + title +
    descLength + desc. ClassicUO'nun okumaya calistigi clilocId
    degerleri "title byte length" sayisal degerine dusuyor,
    client text rendering istemedigi gibi birlesiyor.
  - Yeni (ServUO AddBuffPacket kopyasi): serial + iconId + type
    + fill(4) + iconId + type + fill(4) + duration + fill(3) +
    titleCliloc(4) + secondaryCliloc(4) + args block:
      - args yoksa: fill(10)
      - varsa: fill(4) + 0x0001 + fill(2) + "\t{text}" + null +
        0x0001 + fill(2)
  - Generic title cliloc olarak 1114778 kullaniliyor (ServUO'nun
    dinamik metin icin tercih ettigi cliloc; args icinde gelen
    "\t" prefix'li string literal olarak gosterilir).
  / Layout rewritten to match ServUO AddBuffPacket (Scripts/Misc/
    BuffIcons.cs:432). Payload now contains two 4-byte cliloc
    IDs plus a unicode args block instead of our raw length-
    prefixed text fields.

NOT: Buff ikonunun ekranda gorunmesi icin ClassicUO'da Buff Bar
gump'inin acik olmasi gerekiyor (client-side UI ayari — server
paketi dogru gelse de gump kapaliysa goruntulenmez).
/ The Buff Bar gump in ClassicUO must be open for the icon to
render — even with a valid packet on the wire, a closed gump
just stores the buff silently in the player's internal list.


[2026-04-18] - Buff / curse / paralyze / reflect mekanik butunlestirmesi
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Buff ve debuff buyuleri flag set etmenin otesine gectiler: stat
  artislari/eksilmeleri takip edilip DURATION bitiminde geri
  aliniyor, Paralyze/Invisibility artik sinirli sureli, Magic
  Reflect gelen ilk zararli buyuyu kaynagina iade ediyor, Reactive
  Armor yakin dovusten gelen hasarin 25%'ini saldirgana yansitiyor,
  Protection cast-interrupt sansini yariya indiriyor.

  Buffs/debuffs moved beyond flag-setting: stat deltas are tracked
  and reverted when DURATION expires, Paralyze and Invisibility
  now have a duration, Magic Reflect bounces the first harmful
  spell back to the caster, Reactive Armor reflects 25% of melee
  damage, Protection halves cast-interrupt chance.

ACTIVEEFFECT / ACTIVEEFFECT:
  - Eski tuple (Character, SpellType, long) yerine sinif:
    StrDelta / DexDelta / IntDelta + OldLightLevel + LightChanged
    + AppliedFlag alanlari.
  - ScheduleEffectExpiry: yeni ActiveSpellEffect dondurur. Re-cast
    onceki kaydin deltalarini revert eder, sonra yeni kayit
    acilir — stack degil refresh + temiz reset.
  - RevertDeltas: tum alanlari atomik geri alir (stat -=, flag
    clear, light restore + 0x4E refresh). ProcessExpirations ve
    refresh path'i ayni koddan gecer.
  / ActiveSpellEffect class replaces the tuple; records stat
    deltas, old light level, and applied flag so RevertDeltas can
    undo exactly what was done.

BUFF/CURSE DELTALARI / BUFF/CURSE DELTAS:
  - ApplyBuff artik instance metodu: Strength / Agility / Cunning /
    Bless ScheduleEffectExpiry ile effect olusturup StrDelta,
    DexDelta, IntDelta'yi kaydeder ve stat'i arttirir.
  - ApplyCurse ayni sekilde: Weaken / Clumsy / Feeblemind / Curse
    eksi delta kaydeder ve stat'i azaltir.
  - Bitince stat'lar orijinal degere donuyor; save/reload bundan
    etkilenmiyor (runtime-only effect).
  / ApplyBuff / ApplyCurse now record per-stat deltas via
    ScheduleEffectExpiry so stats revert cleanly on expiration.
    Previous implementation left stats permanently modified.

DUPLICATE FLAG SET KALDIRILDI / DUPLICATE FLAG SET REMOVED:
  - ReactiveArmor / Protection / MagicReflect ApplyBuff'ta flag
    set ediyordu, sonra tekrar ApplySpecificSpell'de ayni flag'i
    set ediyordu. ApplyBuff'taki dallar cikartildi; yalnizca
    ApplySpecificSpell'deki yeni kayit + AppliedFlag ile calisir.
  / Removed duplicate flag-set paths in ApplyBuff that ran for the
    same spells also handled in ApplySpecificSpell.

PARALYZE / INVISIBILITY SURESI:
  - Paralyze: Freeze bayragi DURATION kadar set; artik sonsuz
    donuk kalinmiyor.
  - Invisibility: Invisible bayragi DURATION kadar set; etkinin
    kendiliginden sona ermesi.
  - Ikisi de ScheduleEffectExpiry uzerinden AppliedFlag ile
    isleniyor.
  / Paralyze and Invisibility now use AppliedFlag + duration
    instead of permanently tagging the mobile.

MAGIC REFLECT / MAGIC REFLECT:
  - ApplyCharEffect giris kontrolu: zararli buyu (Damage veya
    Curse flag'li) Reflection'li bir hedefe gelirse, flag
    tuketilir, caster ve target yer degistirir. Tek kullanimlik —
    saldirgan da Reflection'liysa "re-reflect" olmuyor.
  - _activeEffects icindeki MagicReflect kaydi da kaldiriliyor
    ki expire'da ayrica flag clear edilmeye calisilmasin.
  / First harmful spell against a Reflection target bounces back
    to the caster; the flag is consumed and its active-effect
    entry purged so the timer doesn't try to clear it twice.

REACTIVE ARMOR / REACTIVE ARMOR:
  - CombatEngine.ResolveAttack sonunda: hedef Reactive bayrakli
    ise uygulanan hasarin 25%'i saldirgana iletiliyor.
  - Sadece yakin dovus yolunu kapsar; spell hasari
    ApplyCharEffect uzerinden gittigi icin burada yansimaz (magic
    reflect zaten onu karsiliyor).
  / ResolveAttack reflects 25% of dealt physical damage back to
    the attacker if the target has StatFlag.Reactive set. Spell
    damage is excluded — it goes through a different path that
    Magic Reflect covers.

PROTECTION / PROTECTION:
  - TryInterruptFromDamage: caster Protection'li ise (ArcherCanMove
    bayragi, flag reuse) hesaplanan interrupt sansi yariya
    iner. Protection icin ayri bir StatFlag tanimlanmadi; reuse
    kod yorumunda aciklandi.
  / TryInterruptFromDamage halves computed chance when the caster
    carries the Protection flag (ArcherCanMove bit reused).


[2026-04-18] - Buyu suresi / personal light / ParseCurve duzeltmeleri
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Night Sight cast'te efekt + ses geliyordu ama ekran aydinlanmiyordu:
  personal light paketi (0x4E) hic gonderilmiyordu ve DURATION da
  parse edilemedigi icin tum buff'lar fiilen ebedi kaliyordu. Uc
  ayri hata birlestirilince cozuldu — (1) ParseCurve Sphere expr'
  larini (3*60.0) okuyamiyordu, (2) DURATION birim donusumu (script
  seconds -> internal tenths) kayipti, (3) SpellEngine expiration
  altyapisi hic yoktu.

  Casting Night Sight played the effect and sound but left the
  screen dark: the 0x4E PacketPersonalLight was never sent and
  DURATION never parsed, so every buff was effectively permanent.
  Three separate bugs were fixed together: (1) ParseCurve rejected
  Sphere curve expressions like "3*60.0", (2) DURATION unit was not
  converted from script seconds to internal tenths, (3) SpellEngine
  had no expiration infrastructure.

PARSECURVE / PARSECURVE:
  - int.TryParse yerine Sphere script tarzi curve term
    degerlendirme: ondalik / zincirlenmis *, / operatorlerini
    destekliyor. "3*60.0", "1.5*60", "0.5*10" gibi ifadeleri integer
    sonuca ceviriyor. Eski kod asterisk veya nokta gorunce 0
    veriyordu, DurationBase/Scale her buff'ta 0 kaliyordu.
  / ParseCurve now evaluates Sphere-style curve terms (decimal
    literals + chained * /) instead of a plain int.TryParse.

DURATION BIRIMI / DURATION UNIT:
  - Script konvansiyonu saniye, dahili storage onda-saniye
    (CAST_TIME ile tutarli). DefinitionLoader DURATION case'i
    ParseCurve sonucunu x10 ile tenths'e ceviriyor.
  / Script DURATION is in seconds, internal storage is tenths of
    a second (matching CAST_TIME). The DURATION case now multiplies
    by 10 at parse time.

SPELLENGINE EXPIRATION / SPELLENGINE EXPIRATION:
  - Yeni private List<(Character, SpellType, long)> _activeEffects.
  - ScheduleEffectExpiry(caster, target, spell, def): caster'in
    primary skill'ine gore SpellDef.GetDuration cagriyor, tick
    bazinda expire zamanini listeye ekliyor. Ayni (target, spell)
    icin varsa yeniliyor (stack degil, refresh).
  - ProcessExpirations(long now): gecen entry'leri kaldirir,
    UndoEffect cagirir. Program.cs _world.OnTick() sonrasinda
    cagiriyor (hem tek-thread hem multicore pipeline'inda).
  - UndoEffect: NightSight icin stat flag clear + LightLevel=0 +
    OnPersonalLightChanged. ReactiveArmor / Protection / Incognito /
    MagicReflect icin stat flag clear (gercek mekanikleri hala
    eksik ama artik kalici degil).
  / Runtime-only expiration queue on SpellEngine, walked once per
    world tick from Program.cs. Re-cast refreshes the timer rather
    than stacking. UndoEffect per-spell restores state.

NIGHTSIGHT / NIGHTSIGHT:
  - SpellEngine case: target.LightLevel = 30 + OnPersonalLightChanged
    callback + ScheduleEffectExpiry. LightLevel=0 client tarafinda
    "no override" anlamina geliyordu — ServUO konvansiyonuna gore
    daha yuksek = daha parlak, 30 tipik gece global'ini (~12)
    ezmeye yetiyor.
  - SpellEngine.OnPersonalLightChanged event'i (Action<Character>).
    Program.cs target karakterin GameClient'ini bulup
    SendPersonalLight cagiriyor.
  - GameClient.SendPersonalLight(): public metot, mevcut
    Character.LightLevel'i 0x4E paketiyle gonderir. Login /
    resync path'iyle ayni yerden.
  / NightSight now sets LightLevel=30 (script bright override),
    fires OnPersonalLightChanged, Program.cs dispatches to the
    target's GameClient.SendPersonalLight which emits 0x4E. When
    the DURATION timer fires, UndoEffect reverts LightLevel=0 and
    clears the stat flag.

[2026-04-18] - ServUO hareket algoritmasi portu + tiledata entry boyutu fix
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Hareket kontrolu ServUO MovementImpl'in bire bir portuna gecirildi (4-kose
  land Z, surface stack yurutmesi, PersonHeight/StepHeight, diagonal cift-
  kenar kurali). Birlikte kok neden: TileDataReader item entry'sinde
  ReadUInt16+ReadByte (3 byte) okunuyordu; ServUO ReadInt32 (4 byte). Kayma
  her tile'da birikip 0x738'e gelindiginde flag byte'lari tamamen kaymis
  oluyordu — bu yuzden Surface/Bridge static'leri hareket algoritmasinda
  gecersiz seninliyordu, Z desync ve "kare atlamalari" buradan geliyordu.

  Movement checks switched to a verbatim port of ServUO's MovementImpl
  (4-corner land Z, full surface-stack walk, PersonHeight/StepHeight,
  diagonal double-edge rule). Root cause found in parallel: the item-table
  reader in TileDataReader was 1 byte short per entry (ReadUInt16+ReadByte
  vs ServUO's ReadInt32), so every tile past the first had scrambled flag
  bits. Surface/Bridge statics parsed invalid → movement rejected valid
  steps, which is what produced the long-standing Z desync and "square
  jumping" under running.

TILEDATA READER FIX / TILEDATA READER FIX:
  - ItemTileData entry boyutu flagSize+31 -> flagSize+33. Pre-HS 37 byte,
    HS 41 byte — ServUO Server/TileData.cs ile bire bir.
  - Anim alani ReadUInt16+ReadByte yerine ReadUInt32 ile okunuyor; ustteki
    16 bit hala Animation olarak aliniyor.
  / Item entry size corrected to flagSize+33 (37 pre-HS, 41 HS). Anim read
    as Int32 to match ServUO; low 16 bits still exposed as Animation.

HAREKET ALGORITMASI / MOVEMENT ALGORITHM:
  - Yeni: SphereNet.Game.Movement.ServUOMovement — MovementImpl.Check +
    GetStartZ + IsOk portu. CheckMovement(mover, loc, dir, out newZ).
  - Forward + sol/sag kosegen kenarlarda IsOk kafa-carpisma testi; non-GM
    oyuncular icin ikinci kenar zorunlu (kose kesme engeli).
  - Per-tile surface stack: land / static / in-world item adaylari tek tek
    degerlendirilir, mover.Z'ye en yakin olani secilir.
  - MovementEngine.TryMove artik ServUOMovement.CheckMovement cagiriyor;
    eski MaxClimbHeight=12 + IsPassable yolu kaldirildi.
  - CanWalkTo (pathing/AI/teleport) da ayni algoritma uzerinden — tutarli.
  - Turn-in-place TryMove'dan paket handler'a (HandleMove) tasindi: yon
    farkli ise ACK + seq++ + yakinda olanlara bildir, CheckMovement cagirma.
  / New ServUOMovement: Check/GetStartZ/IsOk ported. Double-edge diagonal
    check. Turn-in-place lives in GameClient.HandleMove now so TryMove /
    CanWalkTo are pure "step to adjacent tile" for AI and pathing callers.

MAPDATA HELPERS / MAPDATA HELPERS:
  - MapDataManager.GetAverageZ(mapId, x, y, out low, out center, out top):
    4-kose land ortalamasi (Map.GetAverageZ portu).
  - MapDataManager.IsLandIgnored(tileId): void tile listesi (ServUO
    LandTile.Ignored).
  / Added 4-corner GetAverageZ and IsLandIgnored matching ServUO Map/LandTile.

LAND IMPASSABLE GEVSETMESI / LAND IMPASSABLE RELAXED:
  - Eskisi: landBlocks = land.Impassable.
  - Yeni: landBlocks = land.Impassable && land.Wet (sadece derin su).
  - Neden: bazi stock tiledata.mul kayitlarinda dekoratif slope/rock dokusu
    Impassable isaretli ama client orada yurumeye izin veriyor. Gercek
    duvarlar static olarak modellendigi icin zaten IsOk ile bloklaniyor.
  / landBlocks now requires both Impassable and Wet (deep water only).
    Stock tiledata marks some walkable slope textures as Impassable; real
    walls are static items, which IsOk still enforces.

HAREKET TANISI / MOVEMENT DIAGNOSTICS:
  - Reject logu: reason (forward_blocked / diagonal_edge / mob_block) +
    startZ/startTop/fwdZ + forward tile land geometri + static toplami +
    impassable sayisi + yuzey candidate sayisi + her static icin
    "0x{id}@{z}h{h}f0x{flags}'{name}'" dump'i.
  - ServUOMovement.CheckMovementDetailed -> Diagnostic record. Stale
    IsPassable + staticsBlock dump kaldirildi.
  / Detailed reject telemetry: stage, startZ, forward-tile land + full
    static dump with flags + names; replaces the stale IsPassable-era log.

WALK SEQ RESET / WALK SEQ RESET:
  - GameClient.SendSelfRedraw ve ResyncPosition sonunda
    NetState.WalkSequence = 0 ve _nextMoveTime = 0.
  - 0x20 DrawPlayer client'in walk sayacini sifirlatiyor; server takip
    etmezse sonraki walk seq_mismatch ile reddediliyordu (.invis, mount
    sync, map change dahil her resync'te).
  / After 0x20 DrawPlayer, client resets its walk counter; server now
    mirrors that reset on SelfRedraw / ResyncPosition. Previously any
    resync (invis toggle, mount sync, map change) produced a seq_mismatch
    reject storm on the next client walk.

LOGIN Z DUZELTMESI / LOGIN Z CORRECTION:
  - Kaydedilen Z ile GetEffectiveZ arasindaki fark -RoofSnapTolerance (5)
    ile 0 arasinda ise yukari/asagi snap ediliyor. Ustunde ise catida/
    ust katta oldugu varsayilip dokunulmuyor.
  / Login Z now snaps to nearest surface when stale Z differs from
    terrainZ by <= 5; above that threshold treat as legitimate upper floor.

KALDIRILAN ESKI KOD / REMOVED DEAD CODE:
  - MovementEngine: MaxClimbHeight sabiti, eski PersonHeight sabit, eski
    IsPassable/MaxClimbHeight yolu.
  - GameClient: eski "reason=collision" diag (passable=True
    staticsBlock=0..) — yanlis algoritmadan veri dokumuydu.
  / MovementEngine's legacy climb/passable path and GameClient's
    collision-log-from-wrong-algorithm both removed.

TEST SONUCLARI / TEST RESULTS:
  - 79/79 test gecti (movement + pathfinder + game system + network +
    persistence + scripting + core).
  - PathfinderTests.FindPath_PathLengthCapped: eski MaxPath=24 asumasyonu
    yeni MaxPath=256'ya gore guncellendi (onceden breakpoint'te kalmisti).
  / 79/79 tests green. Pathfinder cap expectation updated from old 24 to

[2026-04-18] - Save dizini temizligi: .bak yok, rolling, hesap formati, UI duzeltme
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Save directory now shows one live file per logical entity — no .bak
  sidecars, no stale shard leftovers. Single-file saves keep the classic
  Sphere layout; Sphere-style size-based rolling (SAVESHARDSIZEMB) opens a
  new file when the current one fills up. Account files obey the same
  SaveFormat abstraction as world saves.

  Save klasoru artik her mantiksal dosya icin tek canli kopya tutuyor;
  .bak dosyasi yok, eski shard artigi temizleniyor. Tek dosya save'lerde
  klasik Sphere yerlesimi korunur; SAVESHARDSIZEMB ile Sphere tarzi
  boyut-tabanli rolling — dosya dolunca yenisi acilir. Hesap dosyalari
  da ayni SaveFormat soyutlamasini kullaniyor.

.BAK KALDIRILDI / .BAK REMOVED:
  - CommitFile artik atomic File.Move(tmp, final, overwrite:true).
  - Eski run'lardan kalan .bak dosyalari bir sonraki save'de otomatik
    siliniyor (RemoveStaleSiblings).
  - Dosya sayisi yariya dusuyor (14 -> 7 tek karakterli mini world icin).
  / CommitFile uses atomic overwrite; old .bak files auto-removed.
    File count drops ~50%.

SIZE-BASED ROLLING:
  - Yeni config: SAVESHARDSIZEMB (default 0 = kapali).
  - SAVESHARDS=1 + SAVESHARDSIZEMB>0: tek dosyayla basla, limit asilinca
    {base}.1.{ext}, {base}.2.{ext} olarak yenisini ac.
  - Tek dosyaya sigarsa: klasik {base}{ext}, manifest yok — Sphere
    davranisi.
  - Limit asilirsa: {base}.0{ext}, {base}.1{ext} + manifest.
  - ISaveWriter.WrittenBytes counter: StreamWriter'in 64KB ic tamponundan
    bagimsiz dogru byte sayimi; KB threshold'larda bile guvenilir.
  / New SAVESHARDSIZEMB config; small worlds stay single-file (classic
    Sphere layout), large worlds auto-roll. Writer-level byte counter
    independent of StreamWriter's internal 64KB buffer.

HESAP DOSYASI / ACCOUNT FILE:
  - AccountManager.Save/Load kaldirildi; persistence Game katmaninda degil.
  - Yeni: SphereNet.Persistence/Accounts/AccountPersistence.cs (static).
  - Dosya uzantisi SaveFormat'a gore: .scp / .scp.gz / .sbin / .sbin.gz.
  - AccountPersistence.Save eski formattaki dosyayi format degisince siler.
  - Legacy [ACCOUNT alice] section header korunur (mevcut .scp uyumlu).
  - AccountManager.AddLoaded(Account) public API eklendi (loader injection).
  / AccountManager delegates persistence to SphereNet.Persistence; single
    live file per format; legacy section header preserved for compat.

CONSOLEFORM UI:
  - Server Status: CPU -> RAM -> world (Items/Chars/Scripts) -> account
    (Accounts/Players Online) -> Uptime (altta). "SERVER STATUS" basligi
    kaldirildi, dogrudan CPU satiriyla basliyor.
  - Quick Actions basligi kaldirildi; 3 buton (DEBUG/RESYNC/SAVE) direk
    panelde. Panel yuksekligi 180 -> 156 (title chrome 35px gitti).
  - StatsCard yuksekligi 430 -> 345 (470 overflow yapip SAVE butonunu
    ekrandan disariya itiyordu).
  / Reordered stats card, removed card titles, fixed clipped SAVE button.

TEST:
  - 17 test (4 yeni account roundtrip + 1 format-switch + mevcut 12).
  / 17 tests (4 account roundtrip + 1 format switch + 12 existing).

CONFIG:
  - SAVESHARDSIZEMB (sphere.ini): size-based rolling threshold MB.

[2026-04-18] - Save formati secimi + shard + binary + migration
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Dunya kaydi artik 4 formatta yazilabilir: klasik .scp metin (default),
  .scp.gz gzip, .sbin tag-stream binary, .sbin.gz binary+gzip. SaveShards
  ile kayit 1-16 parcaya bolunebilir; her shard kendi Task'inda yazilir
  (paralel I/O). Loader dosya uzantisindan formati otomatik alglar, farkli
  snapshot'lar ayni dizinde birlikte bulunabilir. Mevcut .scp save'leri
  hicbir degisiklik olmadan yuklenir (Text/1 default).

  World saves can now be written in 4 formats: classic .scp text (default),
  .scp.gz gzip, .sbin tag-stream binary, .sbin.gz binary+gzip. SaveShards
  splits the save into 1-16 shards written in parallel Tasks. Loader
  auto-detects format from file extension — mixed snapshots coexist safely.
  Existing .scp saves load unchanged (Text/1 default).

YENI DOSYALAR / NEW FILES:
  - SphereNet.Core/Configuration/SaveFormat.cs
  - SphereNet.Persistence/Formats/ISaveIO.cs (ISaveWriter + ISaveReader)
  - SphereNet.Persistence/Formats/TextSaveWriter/Reader.cs (classic .scp)
  - SphereNet.Persistence/Formats/BinarySaveWriter/Reader.cs
      (magic "SNBW", v1, length-prefixed key-value envelope)
  - SphereNet.Persistence/Formats/SaveIO.cs
      (factory: format <-> extension mapping, GZip wrapping)
  - SphereNet.Persistence/Formats/ShardManifest.cs
      ({base}.manifest sidecar + FNV-1a UID hashing for deterministic
      shard placement)
  - SphereNet.Tests/SaveFormatTests.cs (10 tests, 7 format x shard combos)

REFACTOR:
  - WorldSaver: yeni Format + ShardCount property'leri, paralel shard
    yazimi, stale sibling file cleanup (format/shard downgrade sonrasi
    orphan dosya birakmaz), atomic commit (.tmp -> .bak -> final).
  - WorldLoader: auto-detect (manifest varsa shard, yoksa uzanti probe).
    Streaming materialize + SuppressDirtyNotify korunur (million-entity
    yuklerde GC pressure'i onler).

CONFIG (sphere.ini):
  - SAVEFORMAT = Text | TextGz | Binary | BinaryGz (default: Text)
  - SAVESHARDS = 1-16 (default: 1)

KOMUTLAR / COMMANDS:
  .SAVEFORMAT <fmt> [shards]   Owner+ — format degistir + anlik save tetikle
                              (ornekler: .SAVEFORMAT BinaryGz 8,
                               .SAVEFORMAT Text 1)
  Komut once mevcut formati okur, sonra yeni formatta yazar, eski
  dosyalari temizler — tek adimda migration.
  Load current, write new, cleanup old — one-shot migration.

TAHMINI ETKI / EXPECTED IMPACT (500K item + 400K char):
  Text (current)           ~3s save, 150MB disk
  TextGz                   ~3s save,  ~20MB disk
  Text + shard=8           ~500ms save, 150MB disk
  Binary                   ~1s save,   ~80MB disk
  BinaryGz + shard=8       ~300ms save, ~12MB disk

UYUMLULUK / COMPATIBILITY:
  - Eski .scp save'leri loader tarafindan degisiklik olmadan okunur.
  - Default (Text/1) davranisi pre-refactor ile birebir ayni.
  - Sphere/Source-X legacy import yolu etkilenmez.

[2026-04-18] - Stress-test harness / Stress-test harness
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Buyuk olcekli yuk testi icin StressTestEngine eklendi. Britannia'nin
  8 buyuk sehri (Britain, Minoc, Yew, Vesper, Trinsic, Moonglow, Skara
  Brae, Magincia) icine rastgele item+NPC populasyonu scatter eder. Her
  tick batch olarak uretir, STRESS_TEST tag ile isaretler, temizlerken
  tagli objeleri siler. Uretim sirasi ve temizleme ilerlemesini server
  log'una yazar.

  StressTestEngine added for large-scale load testing. Scatters random
  items + NPCs across 8 major towns on map 0 in per-tick batches, tags
  them for cleanup, and logs progress + runtime metrics. Generation and
  deletion are cooperative (no main-loop stalls).

KOMUTLAR / COMMANDS:
  .stress [items] [npcs]  Owner+ — queue generation (default 3M/750K)
  .stressreport           Counsel+ — dump runtime metrics
  .stressclean            Owner+ — queue cleanup of STRESS_TEST tagged

METRIKLER / METRICS:
  - Dunya: chars, items, toplam obje / World: char/item/object counts
  - Bellek: WorkingSet, ManagedHeap, Committed / Memory sections
  - GC: Gen0/Gen1/Gen2 sayisi + son pause / collection counts + last pause
  - CPU: toplam process zamani, thread sayisi / total process time, threads
  - Uretim/temizlik ilerlemesi 5 saniyede bir log'a / Progress every 5s

BATCH BUTCELEri / BATCH BUDGETS:
  - Uretim: 5000 item + 1000 NPC / tick (~24K item/sn, ~4K NPC/sn)
  - Cleanup: 20000 delete / tick

[2026-04-18] - Sync, mount, map ve collision duzeltmeleri / Sync, mount, map and collision fixes
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Iki client arasi gorunurluk, binek, hareket ve map yukleme ile ilgili cok
  sayida duzeltme. Buyuk bir debug oturumunun sonucu. Asagidaki liste oturum
  boyunca tanimlanan ve cozulen sorunlari kapsar.

  Large set of fixes for two-client visibility, mount behaviour, movement and
  map loading. Result of a long debug session. The list below covers every
  issue surfaced and addressed during the session.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:

  [Gorunurluk / Visibility]
  - GameClient.BuildViewDelta: Source-X plevel-gorunurluk kurali — Counsel+
    staff kendinden esit/dusuk plevel karakterlerin invis/hidden halini
    "ghostly" (hue 0x4001) olarak gorur. AllShow override olarak kalir.
    Source-X plevel visibility rule — Counsel+ staff sees hidden/invisible
    characters of equal-or-lower plevel as ghostly. AllShow acts as override.
  - Offline oyuncu karakterleri artik SADECE AllShow ile gorunur. Onceden
    Owner plevel her offline karakteri ghost olarak goruyordu — server
    restart sonrasi "karakter hala oyunda" hissine neden oluyordu.
    Offline players only visible via AllShow. Previously any Owner-plevel
    viewer would see every logged-out player as a ghost, causing the
    "character is still in world after restart" bug.
  - HasKnownChar guard (Fix 2): BroadcastMoveNearby artik sadece zaten
    known mobile'lara 0x77 gonderir. Yeni-range'e giren mobile icin view
    delta 0x78 gonderir — duplicate 0x77/0x78 race'i onlenir.
    BroadcastMoveNearby only sends 0x77 to receivers that already know the
    moving mobile. New-in-range mobiles get 0x78 via the view delta —
    eliminates duplicate packet race.

  [Map ve AREADEF / Map and AREADEF]
  - ResolveAreaDef artik karakterin current map'ini tercih eder. Ayni isimde
    birden fazla AREADEF (ornegin Britain map0 + map1) varsa istenmeyen
    map gecisi olmaz.
    ResolveAreaDef now prefers the caller's current map when multiple
    AREADEFs share a name (e.g. Britain on map0 vs map1).
  - .GO komutu 4. parametre olarak map kabul eder (.go x y z m).
    .GO accepts optional map as 4th argument.
  - OnCharacterMapChanged event: map-bolundugu teleport'ta owner client'a
    PacketMapChange (0xBF sub 0x08) + full Resync gonderilir.
    OnCharacterMapChanged event: on cross-map teleport, owner client
    receives PacketMapChange + full resync.
  - MapDataManager fail-fast: eksik tiledata.mul / multi.idx / multi.mul /
    mapN (mul ya da UOP) / staidxN.mul / staticsN.mul dosyalarinda
    FileNotFoundException atilir, server baslamaz. Sessiz fail + collision
    bozulmasi sorununu onler.
    MapDataManager throws FileNotFoundException on missing UO client data
    so the server refuses to start instead of silently disabling collision.
  - StaticReader MemoryMappedFile pattern'ina tasindi (UopMapReader ile
    tutarlilik, OS paging ile daha az RAM).
    StaticReader migrated to MemoryMappedFile (consistent with UopMapReader).

  [Z ve hareket / Z and movement]
  - MapDataManager.GetEffectiveZ climb-limit filtresi: ulasilamayacak
    yuksekteki surface'lar (ornegin bina catisi Z=30) gorusezilmez olarak
    dondurulmez. "Bineksiz kare atlama" bug'i duzeldi.
    GetEffectiveZ filters surfaces beyond MaxClimbHeight (12) — fixes the
    "square-jumping" MoveReject stutter while running.
  - Pathfinder: her tile icin Z MapData.GetEffectiveZ ile hesaplanir
    (once current.Z her tile icin ayni sayiliyordu, path bulunamiyordu).
    MaxNodes 512 -> 20000, MaxPathLength 24 -> 256.
    Pathfinder now resolves Z per-tile via GetEffectiveZ; limits raised.

  [Binek / Mount]
  - Mount range check (1 tile): Uzaktaki bineklere double-click artik "That
    is too far away." mesaji verir. Uzun mesafe mount'un "karakter binege
    isinlandi" gorselini onler.
    Mount distance check (1 tile) — rejects far-away mounts with a system
    message.
  - EnsureMountedState: login sonrasi mount NPC'si rider pozisyonuyla
    senkronize edilir. Eski kayitlardan gelen stale NPC pozisyonlari
    duzeltilir.
    EnsureMountedState syncs mount NPC position to rider on login.
  - Dismount MoveReject: binek rider.Position'a konur VE client rider
    pozisyonuna snap edilir. Running-dismount'ta karakter 1 tile geri
    kayabilir ama binek her zaman ayak altinda cikar.
    Dismount snaps client to server rider.Position via MoveReject — horse
    always spawns under the rider.

  [INVIS / ALLMOVE komutlari]
  - .INVIS artik argumanli (Source-X uyumlu): .invis 1 = set, .invis 0 =
    clear, .invis (arg yok) = toggle. Onceden her cagri toggle yapiyordu,
    ".invis 0" bile karakteri gorunmez yapabiliyordu.
    .INVIS now argument-aware: 1=set, 0=clear, blank=toggle.
  - INVIS sonrasi sistem mesaji + OnCharacterSelfRedraw event — owner
    client kendi karakterini yari-seffaf (flag=0x80) gorur.
    INVIS emits system message + OnCharacterSelfRedraw so the owner client
    re-renders itself translucent.
  - Character.AllMove runtime-only flag + .ALLMOVE komutu (Counsel+).
    CanWalkTo ve CanShove artik sadece GM+ AllMove aktifken collision'i
    bypass eder — staff karakteri default collision'a tabi.
    Character.AllMove runtime flag + .ALLMOVE command. CanWalkTo/CanShove
    only bypass collision when GM+ has AllMove on.

  [Diagnostik / Diagnostics]
  - .STATICS komutu: karakterin oldugu tile'daki statik listesini ve her
    birinin Impassable/Surface/Wall flag'lerini yazar — collision bug
    tanilari icin.
    .STATICS command: lists statics + flags at the character's tile.
  - OnSysMessage handler'i artik server log'una da yazar — .statics/.where
    gibi komutlarin ciktilari 0xAE paketini decode etmeden log'dan okunur.
    OnSysMessage handler now also writes to the server log.

  [Logout]
  - PacketLogoutRequest (0xD1 incoming) + PacketLogoutAck (0xD1 outgoing):
    UO client "karakter secim ekranina don" istegini isler. Server
    OnDisconnect flow'unu calistirir, nearby'lara DeleteObject gonderir,
    IsOnline=false yapar. Onceden bu paket hic handle edilmiyordu —
    karakter dunyada "takili" kaliyordu.
    PacketLogoutRequest/Ack (0xD1): handles "return to character select".
    Previously unhandled, leaving characters stuck in-world.

  [Altyapi / Infrastructure]
  - DIAGNOSTIC fast-path view-delta (Plan B) eklendi: main loop'ta
    HasDirty gated olarak view update + DrainDirty. Suan devre disi
    (FastPathViewDeltaEnabled=false) — tekrar aktive etmek isterseniz
    Program.cs icindeki tek satiri degistirin.
    DIAGNOSTIC fast-path view-delta (Plan B) added but currently disabled —
    flip the flag in Program.cs to re-enable.
  - GameWorld.HasDirty O(1) accessor eklendi.
    Added GameWorld.HasDirty O(1) accessor.

[2026-04-17] - Z desync, tooltip spam, mount loop duzeltmeleri / Z desync, tooltip spam, mount loop fixes
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Pozisyon desync duzeltildi: sunucu Z'si GetEffectiveZ ile hesaplaniyor ama
  MoveAck (0x22) pozisyon bilgisi tasimiyordu — client kendi Z tahminini
  kullaniyordu. Simdi Z degistiginde DrawPlayer (0x20) ile duzeltme gonderiliyor.
  BroadcastDrawObject artik _lastKnownPos'u guncelliyor (teleport/mount/resurrect
  sonrasi duplicate 0x77 onlendi). 0xDC tooltip spam duzeltildi — cache hit'te
  artik hicbir paket gonderilmiyor (onceden her istek icin 0xDC gonderiyordu).
  Binek ustundeyken mountable NPC'ye cift tiklamak artik paperdoll acmiyor,
  "You are already riding." mesaji gosteriyor.

  Position desync fixed: server Z was calculated via GetEffectiveZ but MoveAck
  (0x22) carries no position data — client kept its own predicted Z. Now sends
  DrawPlayer (0x20) correction when Z changes. BroadcastDrawObject now updates
  receiving clients' _lastKnownPos (prevents duplicate 0x77 after teleport/mount/
  resurrect). 0xDC tooltip spam fixed — no packet sent on cache hit (previously
  sent 0xDC for every request). Double-clicking mountable NPC while already
  mounted now shows "You are already riding." instead of opening paperdoll.

  [GameClient.cs — HandleMove]
  - Z correction: hareket sonrasi Z degismisse DrawPlayer (0x20) gonderiliyor

  - BroadcastMoveNearby kullanarak _lastKnownPos guncelleniyor
    Uses BroadcastMoveNearby to update _lastKnownPos on receiving clients

  [GameClient.cs — HandleAOSTooltip]
  - Cache hit'te 0xDC gonderimi kaldirildi (100+ gereksiz paket → 0)
    Removed 0xDC send on cache hit (100+ unnecessary packets → 0)

  - Resurrect broadcast BroadcastMoveNearby kullanarak _lastKnownPos guncelleniyor
    Resurrect broadcast uses BroadcastMoveNearby to update _lastKnownPos

[2026-04-17] - Performans optimizasyonu: container index, cached sayaclar, streaming save / Performance optimization: container index, cached counters, streaming save
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  1M item + 100K char senaryosunda O(N) full-scan darbogazlari giderildi.
  Container lookup, obje sayaclari ve world save islemi optimize edildi.
  Dead code temizligi yapildi. BENCHMARK admin komutu eklendi.
  Removed O(N) full-scan bottlenecks for 1M item + 100K char scenarios.
  Container lookup, object counters and world save optimized.
  Dead code cleaned up. BENCHMARK admin command added.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - Container Reverse Index: GetContainerContents() O(N) full scan yerine
    _containerIndex dictionary ile O(1) lookup. Item.ContainedIn setter'i
    eski/yeni container icin indeksi otomatik guncelliyor.
    Container Reverse Index: GetContainerContents() uses _containerIndex
    dictionary for O(1) lookup instead of O(N) full scan. Item.ContainedIn
    setter automatically updates index for old/new container.
  - Cached TotalChars/TotalItems: Her cagrisinda LINQ .Count() ile 1M obje
    sayan property'ler yerine _totalChars/_totalItems sayaclari eklendi.
    Create/Delete islemlerinde guncelleniyor.
    Cached TotalChars/TotalItems: Added _totalChars/_totalItems counters
    instead of LINQ .Count() scanning 1M objects per call. Updated on
    Create/Delete operations.
  - WorldSaver Streaming: .ToList() ile 1M objeyi snapshot almak yerine
    dictionary uzerinden dogrudan iterate ediliyor (~9MB allokasyon tasarrufu).
    SaveItems/SaveChars imzalari List<ObjBase> -> IEnumerable<ObjBase>.
    WorldSaver Streaming: Direct iteration over dictionary instead of
    .ToList() snapshot of 1M objects (~9MB allocation savings).
    SaveItems/SaveChars signatures changed to IEnumerable<ObjBase>.
  - GetNpcSnapshot dead code temizligi: TimerWheel her zaman mevcut oldugu
    icin GetNpcSnapshot() metodu ve tum fallback dallari silindi.
    _npcTimerWheel nullable turden null! ile degistirildi.
    GetNpcSnapshot dead code cleanup: Removed GetNpcSnapshot() method and
    all fallback branches since TimerWheel is always initialized.
    Changed _npcTimerWheel from nullable to null!.
  - BENCHMARK admin komutu: 1000x container lookup + 10000x counter erisimi
    olcumu. Telnet veya sunucu konsolundan calistirilabilir.
    BENCHMARK admin command: Measures 1000x container lookup + 10000x
    counter access. Can be run from Telnet or server console.
  - README guncellendi: Dahili Optimizasyonlar tablosu ve BENCHMARK komutu
    dokumantasyonu eklendi.
    README updated: Internal Optimizations table and BENCHMARK command
    documentation added.

[2026-04-17] - Multi-versiyon client destegi: paket uyumlulugu / Multi-version client support: packet compatibility
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Farkli client versiyonlari (2.x - 7.x) ile uyumluluk icin paket formatlari
  dinamik hale getirildi. Dusuk versiyonlu client'lar artik TCP stream desync
  yasamadan baglanabilir.
  Packet formats made dynamic for compatibility with different client versions
  (2.x - 7.x). Lower version clients can now connect without TCP stream desync.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - NetState'e versiyon helper property'leri eklendi: IsClientPost6017,
    IsClientPost60142, IsClientPost7090, IsClientPost70180.
    Added version helper properties to NetState.
  - 0x24 (OpenContainer): 7.0.9+ icin 9 byte, eski client'lar icin 7 byte.
    0x24 (OpenContainer): 9 bytes for 7.0.9+, 7 bytes for older clients.
  - 0x25 (ContainerItem): 6.0.1.7+ icin 21 byte (grid index), eski icin 20 byte.
    0x25 (ContainerItem): 21 bytes for 6.0.1.7+ (grid index), 20 bytes for older.
  - 0xB9 (FeatureEnable): 6.0.14.2+ icin 5 byte (uint), eski icin 3 byte (ushort).
    0xB9 (FeatureEnable): 5 bytes (uint) for 6.0.14.2+, 3 bytes (ushort) for older.
  - 0x11 (StatusFull): expansion level client versiyonuna gore belirleniyor
    (0=pre-AOS, 3=AOS, 4=SE, 5=ML).
    0x11 (StatusFull): expansion level determined by client version.
  - Feature flags (0xB9) client versiyonuna gore ayarlaniyor: pre-AOS=0x0000,
    AOS=0x0001, SE=0x0004, ML=0x0044, SA=0x0244.
    Feature flags (0xB9) adjusted per client version.
  - Incoming paket uzunluklari dinamik: 0x08 (DropItem) 14/15 byte,
    0x00 (CreateCharacter) 104/106 byte.
    Dynamic incoming packet lengths: 0x08 (DropItem) 14/15 bytes,
    0x00 (CreateCharacter) 104/106 bytes.
  - NetworkManager paket dispatcher'i versiyon-aware uzunluk kullaniyor.
    NetworkManager packet dispatcher uses version-aware length lookup.

  - src/SphereNet.Network/Packets/Outgoing/ExtendedPackets.cs
  - src/SphereNet.Network/Packets/PacketDefinitions.cs

[2026-04-17] - Login sonrasi donma ve hits/mana 0 duzeltildi / Fix post-login freeze and hits/mana showing 0
----------------------------------------

OZET / SUMMARY:
  Login sonrasi 3-5 adim atinca olusan donma ve client'ta hits/mana 0 gorunme
  sorunu duzeltildi. Uc ana neden tespit ve giderildi.
  Fixed post-login freeze after 3-5 steps and hits/mana displaying as 0 on client.
  Three root causes identified and resolved.

DEGISIKLIKLER / CHANGES:
  - 0x11 (StatusFull) expansion level 3 (AOS) -> 5 (ML) olarak duzeltildi.
    0xB9 feature flags (0x0244 = SA+ML) ile uyumlu hale getirildi. Client artik
    dogru byte offset'lerden okuyarak hits/mana degerlerini gorebilir.
    Fixed 0x11 expansion level from 3 (AOS) to 5 (ML), matching 0xB9 feature flags.
  - 0x11 paket field sirasi duzeltildi: ML->AOS->SE (yanlis) yerine AOS->SE->ML
    (dogru RunUO/standard sirasi). Client artik field'lari dogru offset'lerden okur.
    Fixed 0x11 packet field order from ML->AOS->SE (wrong) to AOS->SE->ML (correct).
  - Login sirasindaki fazla SendDrawObject (0x78) kaldirildi. Resync() zaten
    DrawObject gonderdigi icin ucuncu paket gereksizdi ve client'i bozabiliyordu.
    Removed redundant SendDrawObject after Resync() during login sequence.
  - 0x11 paketi debug log filtresinden cikarildi, hata ayiklamayi kolaylastirir.
    Removed 0x11 from debug log filter to aid packet debugging.
  - 0x24 (OpenContainer) paketi 7 -> 9 byte olarak duzeltildi. 7.0.9+ client'lar
    ekstra 2 byte (container type 0x7D) bekler; eksik byte'lar TCP stream desync'e
    ve client donmasina neden oluyordu.
    Fixed 0x24 packet from 7 to 9 bytes. 7.0.9+ clients expect extra container type
    field; missing bytes caused TCP stream desync and client freeze.
  - 0x25 (ContainerItem) paketi 20 -> 21 byte olarak duzeltildi. 6.0.1.7+ client'lar
    ekstra grid index byte'i bekler; eksik byte ayni stream desync sorununa yol aciyordu.
    Fixed 0x25 packet from 20 to 21 bytes with grid index for 6.0.1.7+ clients.

ETKILENEN DOSYALAR / AFFECTED FILES:
  - src/SphereNet.Network/Packets/Outgoing/ExtendedPackets.cs
  - src/SphereNet.Game/Clients/GameClient.cs
  - src/SphereNet.Network/State/NetState.cs

[2026-04-16] - Script-Driven SPEECH Sistemi
----------------------------------------

YENI OZELLIKLER:
  - NPC konusma sistemi script-driven hale getirildi. [SPEECH spk_xxx] section'lari
    artik parse edilip StoredKeys olarak hafizada tutuluyor. NPC'ler CHARDEF'teki
    SPEECH= veya TSPEECH= ile atanan speech resource'larindaki ON=*keyword* pattern'lerine
    gore konusan oyunculara tepki verebiliyor. (ResourceHolder.cs, CharDef.cs,
    TriggerRunner.cs, TriggerDispatcher.cs, Program.cs)
  - Wildcard pattern matching: *keyword* (contains), keyword* (startsWith),
    *keyword (endsWith), keyword (exact). Tumu case-insensitive.
  - TSPEECH destegi: CharDef'e birden fazla speech resource atanabiliyor (SPEECH +
    TSPEECH). Ilk eslesen pattern'in body'si execute ediliyor.
  - Trigger zinciri: f_onchar_speech -> @NPCHearGreeting -> SPEECH triggers ->
    hardcoded fallback -> @NPCHearUnknown. Geriye uyumluluk korunuyor.
  - ResourceId.FromString(name, type) overload eklendi: Belirli bir ResType ile
    ResourceId olusturma destegi. (ResourceId.cs)

  - SRC.BANKSELF: Oyuncunun bank kutusunu acar. Script'te SPEECH section'larindan
    cagrilabilir (ornegin spk_banker icindeki ON=*bank*). (GameClient.cs)
  - BUY: Vendor buy islemi placeholder'i (tam vendor buy/sell destegiyle
    genisletilecek). (GameClient.cs)
  - BYE: NPC etkilesimini sonlandirir. (GameClient.cs)

[2026-04-16] - Delta View, Paket Duzeltmeleri ve Performans Optimizasyonu
----------------------------------------

KRITIK DUZELTMELER:
  - SendUpdateMobile 0x20->0x77: Diger karakterlerin pozisyon guncellemesi
    PacketDrawPlayer (0x20) yerine PacketMobileMoving (0x77) ile gonderiliyor.
    0x20 paketi istemciye "sen bu karaktersin" diyordu; NPC icin gonderildiginde
    istemci donuyordu. Hareket broadcast, resurrect ve war mode broadcast da
    ayni sekilde duzeltildi. (GameClient.cs, GamePackets.cs)
  - ConsumeDirty: Dirty flag'ler her tick sonunda temizleniyor. Onceden objeler
    bir kez dirty olduktan sonra flag'leri asla sifirlanmiyordu, sonraki property
    degisiklikleri dirty set'e tekrar eklenemiyordu. NPC flickering ve eksik
    goruntulenmelerin temel nedeni buydu. (Program.cs, ObjBase.cs)
  - War mode 0x72 onay paketi: Sunucu istemciye PacketWarModeResponse (0x72)
    gondermiyordu. Istemci bu paketi almadan war mode'a gecmiyordu.
    (GamePackets.cs, GameClient.cs)
  - Login Z duzeltmesi: Karakter zemin altindaysa (Z < terrainZ) otomatik olarak
    terrain yuksekligine tasinir. Zemin ustundeki karakterlere dokunulmaz
    (bina/kopru uzerinde olabilirler). (GameClient.cs)
  - .GO komutu Z otomatik cozumleme: Z belirtilmediginde GetEffectiveZ ile
    terrain yuksekligi hesaplanir (onceden Z=0 ataniyordu). (SpeechEngine.cs)
  - MovementEngine Z duzeltmesi: TryMove hedef pozisyonu icin terrain effectiveZ
    hesaplaniyor (onceden ch.Z kullaniliyordu, karakter haritanin altina
    dusuyordu). (MovementEngine.cs)

YENI PAKETLER:
  - PacketMobileMoving (0x77): Diger karakterlerin pozisyon/yon guncellemesi.
    17 byte sabit boyut. Serial, Body, X, Y, Z, Dir, Hue, Flags, Notoriety.
  - PacketWarModeResponse (0x72): War/peace mode onay paketi.

MOUNT/DISMOUNT:
  - Dismount pozisyon: Binek artik rider'in koordinatina spawn oluyor
    (onceden farkli tile'a yerlestirmeye calisiyordu). (MountEngine.cs)
  - Mount/dismount walk state reset: WalkSequence ve _nextMoveTime sifirlaniyor,
    mount hiz gecislerinde fastwalk reject onleniyor. Dismount'ta rider'a
    PacketDrawPlayer (0x20) gonderimi eklendi. (GameClient.cs)

PERFORMANS:
  - Ana dongu latency: Thread.Sleep(1) -> SpinWait(100) + Thread.Sleep(0).
    Windows'ta Thread.Sleep(1) ~15ms uyuyordu (timer resolution 15.6ms),
    localhost ping 9-10ms'den <1ms'e dustu. (Program.cs)
  - Stat setter change-guard: Hits/Mana/Stam/Direction setter'lari deger
    degismediginde MarkDirty cagirmiyor. Gereksiz dirty set entryleri
    onleniyor. (Character.cs)
  - ApplyDirtyOnly Stats branch: NPC'ler icin Stats-only dirty flag islemesi
    eklendi. (GameClient.cs)

OYUN MEKANIGI:
  - Kosma stamina maliyeti kaldirildi (weight sistemi henuz yok).
    Item agirliklari implement edilince tekrar eklenecek. (MovementEngine.cs)

DOKUMANTASYON:
  - README.md: Performans, WinForms konsol, proje yapisi, oyun dongusu,
    yapilandirma, PerfHarness ve script sistemi bolumleri eklendi.

    iletilmesinin yani sira SphereNet.Host.exe konsol penceresine de yazilir.
    Level'e gore renk kodlamasi: Fatal=kirmizi, Error=koyu kirmizi,
    Warning=sari, Information=gri, Debug/Verbose=koyu gri.
    Host console mirroring: Server stdout/stderr is now written to the
    SphereNet.Host.exe console window in addition to forwarding to the web
    panel. Color-coded by level: Fatal=red, Error=dark red, Warning=yellow,
    Information=gray, Debug/Verbose=dark gray.
  - Thread-safe konsol yazimi: lock(_consoleLock) ile renk degisimi sirasinda
    ciktilarin karismasinin onune gecildi.
    Thread-safe console writes: lock(_consoleLock) prevents interleaved
    output during color changes.


[2026-04-24] - IPC JsonElement fix, log batching, debug toggle runtime, thread count
----------------------------------------

HATA DUZELTMELERI / BUG FIXES:
  - IpcBridge JsonElement use-after-dispose duzeltildi: ProcessMessage'da
    JsonDocument using ile dispose ediliyor, ama TCS ile baska thread'e
    verilen JsonElement gecersiz belleğe isaret ediyordu. d.Clone() ile
    bagimsiz kopya alınarak duzeltildi. Bu hata GetDebugState, account
    sorgulari ve diger IPC query'lerinin null/default donmesine neden
    oluyordu (debug toggle'larin hep OFF gorunmesi dahil).
    IpcBridge JsonElement use-after-dispose fixed: JsonDocument was
    disposed at end of ProcessMessage via using, but the JsonElement
    passed to TCS on another thread pointed to freed memory. Fixed by
    calling d.Clone() to create an independent copy. This bug caused
    GetDebugState, account queries and other IPC queries to return
    null/default (including debug toggles always showing OFF).
  - Panel debug toggle'lari (DebugPackets/ScriptDebug) artik runtime'i
    da guncelliyor: _network.DebugPackets, tum aktif baglanti state'leri,
    _triggerDispatcher.ScriptDebug, _triggerRunner.ScriptDebug ve
    _logLevelSwitch guncelleniyor. Onceki kod sadece _config'e yaziyordu.
    Panel debug toggles (DebugPackets/ScriptDebug) now update runtime
    state too: _network.DebugPackets, all active connection states,
    _triggerDispatcher.ScriptDebug, _triggerRunner.ScriptDebug and
    _logLevelSwitch. Previous code only wrote to _config.

YENI OZELLIKLER / NEW FEATURES:
  - SignalR log batching: PanelLogSink artik gelen loglari buffer'a
    ekliyor ve 150ms arayla toplu gonderiyor (ReceiveLogBatch). Bu
    sunucu baslangicinda yuzlerce log satirinin teker teker gonderilmesi
    yerine tek mesajda gonderilmesini saglar. Frontend logs store'a
    addBatch metodu eklendi.
    SignalR log batching: PanelLogSink now buffers incoming logs and
    flushes every 150ms as a batch (ReceiveLogBatch). This sends hundreds
    of startup log lines in a single message instead of one-by-one.
    Frontend logs store gains addBatch method.
  - Dashboard'a Threads karti eklendi: ServerStats record'una ThreadCount
    alani eklendi. PanelHost StatsLoop'ta Process.Threads.Count ile
    doldurulur.
    Dashboard Threads card added: ThreadCount field added to ServerStats
    record. Populated via Process.Threads.Count in PanelHost StatsLoop.
